Unrest in Changle County, Fujian, Not Settled 60

▲Provincial Troops Have Not Yet Advanced to Suppress

▲Farmers Deeply Regret Being Deceived

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Changle Incident occurred, and as of the 25th, the farmers are still occupying the city. Provincial troops have not yet advanced to suppress. The county chamber of commerce provides meals for the farmers, 60 tables per meal. The merchants and residents are complaining incessantly, so on the 24th, they convened a citizens' meeting, which resolved to support the provincial government's ban on opium seedlings and to oppose the marine corps' levy of opium taxes. It also issued a declaration stating that it would implement the automatic removal of opium seedlings as a promotion for all counties, and would resist with all their might anyone who used force to suppress it. The ships traveling between Changle and Fuzhou resumed sailing on the 24th. Wealthy families in the county, fearing that the provincial troops would advance to suppress and devastate the area, fled to the province with their families. It is said that only more than 300 genuine armed farmers entered the city this time, and the rest were bandits from Chen Wei's troops in the southern township of Fuzhou. Recently, there has been a dark undercurrent due to disputes over the allocation of military pay. On the evening of the 23rd, Chen went to rob Wutian Township, at the border of Fuqing and Changle counties. On the 24th, he intercepted a ship sailing from Fuzhou to Kengtian, taking many people. Lin Zongyue, the commander of the guard group elected by the farmers, did not approve of this situation and wanted to withdraw from the county and defend the northern district, but Chen Wei blocked the north gate, not allowing them to leave. Chen's intention was to have the provincial troops advance to suppress, so that the farmers would have nowhere to go, and then kidnap them to the mountains to expand his own power. At this point, the farmers also deeply regretted cooperating with him and leading him into the city, only to be kidnapped by him. The Li Huan regiment of the Liu Heding division, which was transferred by the provincial government, is now led by Brigade Commander Liu Shangzhi and is advancing to Changle to suppress it. (December 25th)

Hubei in the Past Year 61

▲No Progress in Any Facilities

▲Banditry and Floods Are the Main Causes

Hankou Correspondence: The civil administration, finance, construction, education, and other aspects of Hubei Province in the twentieth year of the Republic of China (1931) have been hindered in their progress by the rampancy of the Red Bandits and the severity of the floods. As the year draws to a close, I will record the general situation of what has transpired as follows:

▲Civil Administration: The Civil Affairs Department has had three changes of director this year. Due to differences in political views, there have inevitably been biases towards certain areas and neglect of others. The first director, Wu Xingya, focused on local autonomy, organizing the baojia system (a system of collective responsibility), and vigorously suppressing banditry. However, due to financial constraints, he was hindered by public opinion and failed to complete his work. Liu Wendao succeeded him as the director of the Civil Affairs Department but failed to continue the unfinished tasks of his predecessor. The current director, Zhu Huaibing, has once again emphasized the suppression of bandits, requiring county magistrates to be responsible for剿匪. Those who are found to be corrupt or harmful to the people will be punished with severe laws. He also pays attention to the reorganization of local defense. Zhu has personally inspected various counties in eastern Hubei and will continue to inspect southern, western, and northern Hubei in order to implement reforms. No other major political initiatives have been proposed.

▲Finance: The financial situation of Hubei Province has long been on the brink of collapse. On New Year's Day of the twentieth year (1931), the government followed orders to abolish the likin tax (a form of internal tariff) and introduced a business tax to compensate for the loss. However, due to poor implementation, the results have been minimal. After the previous director, Zhang Guanshi, left office, Wu Guozhen succeeded him. Wu, who was originally the director of the Hankou Finance Bureau, also found it impossible to cope with the situation after taking office. The Finance Department is supposed to issue funds for bandit suppression, police, administration, and education, which amount to approximately 1.4 to 1.5 million yuan per month, while the income is only one million yuan. In recent months, it has been relying entirely on borrowing to make ends meet. As the end of the year approaches, the situation is even more dire. It is estimated that the income from the Hankou City Tax, business tax, and land tax from various counties totals 300,000 yuan, which is a reliable source of funds. The central government has provided 350,000 yuan, and a special tax subsidy of 456,000 yuan. These funds will not be available at the beginning of the year, and the monthly deficit in the future will be approximately one million yuan. Although Chairman He has proposed the issuance of three new taxes, it is feared that they will be difficult to implement due to practical constraints.

▲Construction: Due to financial difficulties, all kinds of construction projects have been unable to be realized. Even if some construction is carried out, it is only done in a makeshift manner. The Construction Department is essentially a facade. According to the Construction Department's recent report to the provincial representatives' assembly, the most significant achievements include the development of provincial roads, the construction of suburban roads, the establishment of nurseries in various counties, and the implementation of the metric system. However, it especially focused on shipping, mining, and factory construction. However, due to the flood disaster, buildings along the river were destroyed. Therefore, repairing breached embankments, provincial roads, bridge supports, roadbeds, culverts, and restoring agriculture in various counties, as well as promoting afforestation, will be the most important tasks in the future.

▲Education: The authorities in Hubei Province do not neglect education. In addition to Wuhan University, which is a national university, in the first semester of the twentieth year (1931), the provincial Department of Education was in charge of education in the counties, while the municipal Bureau of Education was in charge of education in Hankou. In the second semester, the provincial and municipal governments merged, and the municipal Bureau of Education was incorporated into the provincial Department of Education. The expenses of various schools, libraries, and public education centers were all provided by the provincial Department of Education. The number of students enrolled has increased compared to previous years, but due to financial constraints, it is still difficult to accommodate everyone. In particular, there are too few primary schools, and more than 70% of children are not in school (this is especially true in Hankou City, and the situation is roughly the same elsewhere). Teachers are constantly complaining about their hardships. Currently, the funds for provincial schools have only been issued up to September, and the funds for Hankou schools have been issued up to October. Teachers are constantly complaining about their hardships.

▲Municipal Administration: After Hankou was changed to an ordinary city, He Baohua was appointed as the mayor. Soon after He took office, the city was hit by a flood, and municipal administration could not be started. In particular, the destruction of roads has been criticized by the citizens. Hankou's commerce has been affected by the flood and the decline in public bonds. Its stagnation is unprecedented. Banks are afraid to lend money, and many money houses have collapsed. The special tax, which is known for its vitality and ability to assist commerce, has also become unsustainable because Sichuan goods cannot be transported to Hankou. Under these circumstances, it will be difficult to restore Hankou's prosperity.

▲Disaster Relief: The flood of the twentieth year (1931) was unprecedented in sixty years. The water level of the Yangtze River reached 53.6 feet. Forty-five of the province's sixty-eight counties were affected, covering 169,000 square li, accounting for more than 22% of the total area. The affected population totaled 9.5 million people, accounting for more than 35% of the total population. Wuhan was particularly severely affected, and the number of refugees was also the highest. Although the Provincial Emergency Relief Association, Disaster Relief Branch, and Post-Disaster Relief Committee were established and made every effort to provide relief, refugees were still dying of starvation, cold, and disease everywhere. The Emergency Relief Association and Disaster Relief Branch have now been closed, and the Post-Disaster Relief Committee is handling the post-disaster relief efforts, implementing work relief and agricultural relief separately to provide assistance. However, the province's vitality has been damaged, and Hankou's essence has been exhausted. ▲Bandit Suppression: Banditry in Hubei Province has always been rampant. Kong Helong's gang harasses southern Hubei, while Kuang Jixun's and Xu Jishen's gangs harass eastern Hubei. He Long's and Duan Dechang's gangs harass western and northern Hubei. They suppress each other, and the bandits flee. Among them, He Long's and Kuang Jixun's gangs are the strongest. Therefore, northern and eastern Hubei are particularly severely affected. The initial organization in charge of bandit suppression in the province was the Wuhan Headquarters of the Commander-in-Chief, which has now been changed to the Special Envoy's Pacification Office stationed in Hubei. He Chengjun, the director of the office, is in charge of all national troops stationed in Hubei. He Long's and Duan Dechang's gangs have been surrounded near Zaoshi by Xu Yuanquan's troops and are relatively easy to annihilate. Kong's gang has fled back to Jiangxi Province, and a portion has fled into Hunan Province, where they are being blocked and suppressed by Guo Rudong's and Xie Bin's troops. For now, there is nothing to worry about. However, Kuang's gang is becoming increasingly rampant. Huang'an has been lost, and Zhao Guanying, the commander of the 69th Division, is said to have died in battle. The Pacification Office has dispatched the 33rd Division under Ge Yunlong to advance and suppress the bandits at full speed, which may slightly blunt the bandits' edge.

Re-surveying the Junction of the Yellow River in Hebei, Henan, and Shandong Provinces 62

▲The Ministry of Interior Asks for a Report on the Situation of River Affairs in Shandong

Jinan Correspondence: The lower reaches of the Yellow River in Hebei, Henan, and Shandong provinces are subject to river disasters every year. Although prevention and repair are not easy, there are many reasons for this. One of the long-standing causes is that each province governs itself and there is no overall plan. The purpose of this year's Yellow River Conference is to organize a joint Yellow River Affairs Association of Hebei, Henan, and Shandong provinces to enable the three provinces to jointly study methods for preventing and controlling the Yellow River. The Shandong River Affairs Bureau is currently preparing to convene the River Affairs Bureaus of Hebei and Henan provinces to discuss the methods of organizing the joint association. The issue of the Yellow River provincial boundary, which has been a matter of dispute for many years, is also an unresolved issue. For example, Shandong is located at the lowest reaches of the Yellow River. The upstream provincial boundary is intertwined with those of Hebei and Henan. If a dangerous project is located in Province A and a breach occurs, Province B will suffer. Province A does not want to do its best to defend it because it is not in its own interest, while Province B, although wanting to do its best to defend it, is limited by its administrative boundaries and cannot act beyond its jurisdiction. After repeated delays, the river embankment has breached. Therefore, Shandong has repeatedly requested that the provincial boundary be redrawn. Furthermore, the different organizations and funding of the River Affairs Bureaus in each province also make it difficult to achieve a unified effect. At today's (29th) provincial government meeting, the Secretariat submitted a report stating that the Ministry of Interior had sent a consultation regarding the case of Hebei, Henan, and Shandong provinces sending personnel to re-survey the boundary and requesting a report on the situation and funding of river affairs in Shandong. It was decided to discuss them together and order the Construction Department and River Affairs Bureau to discuss and review them before forwarding them. The Ministry of Interior's consultation is transcribed below: (1) The Yellow River River Affairs Conference, according to the temporary proposal of members Li Shutian, Sun Fushe, Chen Zhansi, etc., requested that the Ministry of Interior revise the boundary near the Yellow River in Henan, Hebei, and Shandong to avoid the interlacing of the Yellow River embankments to facilitate defense. It was resolved to send it to the Ministry of Interior for adoption and implementation. It is recorded in the minutes. The boundary near the Yellow River in Henan, Hebei, and Shandong provinces is intertwined, which causes many obstacles to embankment defense. It should be re-surveyed to facilitate river defense. However, this matter concerns changes in the administrative area of ​​the province. According to the provisions of the Provincial and Municipal County Boundary Survey Regulations and the Outline of the County Administrative Area Consolidation Measures promulgated by the Ministry, all administrative areas that violate the natural terrain of the land and the convenience of administrative management must be effectively consolidated. How should the administrative areas of the counties on both sides of the Yellow River be rectified and redrawn? It is proposed that your provincial government, together with the Hebei Provincial Government, promptly appoint commissioners in accordance with the provisions of Article 8 of the Boundary Survey Regulations to conduct on-site surveys, and then jointly propose a consolidation plan, along with diagrams, and submit it to the Ministry for review and submission to the Executive Yuan for submission to the National Government for approval and promulgation to facilitate administration. In addition to distributing it, it is appropriate to consult and request your consideration and handling, and hope to see a reply. (2) Regarding the Yellow River River Affairs, the Ministry convened representatives of relevant agencies and water conservancy experts at the Ministry's meeting. According to the proposal of the representative of the Henan Provincial Government, the organizational law of the River Affairs Bureau of each province and the measures for clarifying and standardizing the official system of river affairs should be formulated. In addition, the representatives of the Hebei and Henan Provincial Governments jointly proposed to restore the official system of river affairs to emphasize the authority and facilitate implementation. After joint discussion, the principles were approved, and the Ministry of Interior would formulate the organizational measures of the Yellow River River Affairs Bureau and submit them for approval and implementation. The minutes are recorded. The organization of the River Affairs Bureaus in the lower reaches of the Yellow River varies from province to province and should be improved to achieve a unified and consistent effect. However, the organization of the River Affairs Bureau is closely related to the complexity of river works affairs in each province and the amount of confirmed funding. Overall planning is important, but local conditions should also be taken into account. At the beginning of the deliberation, research should be as detailed as possible to avoid obstacles during implementation. Your provincial government should separately ascertain the status of river works affairs in this province, the amount of confirmed funding each year, the current organization of the River Affairs Bureau, the number of prescribed personnel, and the opinions of your provincial government on revising the organization, and propose a reply for reference and verification. In addition to distributing it, it is appropriate to consult and request your consideration and handling.

Prelude to the Alliance of the Five Southwestern Provinces 63

▲Southwestern Provinces Foreign Affairs Association Established in Guangdong

Guangzhou Correspondence: The southwestern provinces have recently realized that, due to the environmental situation, they must unite to deal with the current situation. Since Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi reported that foreigners in Vietnam were disturbing the border of Guangxi, the southwestern authorities have become more justified in carrying out joint actions. Therefore, representatives of the southwestern provinces initiated the establishment of the Preparatory Committee of the Southwestern Provinces Foreign Affairs Association in Guangdong. In the middle of this month, a preparatory meeting was held, and six principles of the association were decided as follows: (1) The Southwest will cooperate and unite against foreign aggression. (2) The National Government is requested to convene a Southwestern Border Defense Conference immediately and establish a Southwestern Border Defense Committee. (3) Request the National Government to prepare military supplies in advance, and build fortresses along the southwestern border and complete southwestern transportation in sections. (4) Actively organize the militias of the southwestern provinces as a backing for the government against foreign aggression. (5) Strictly guard against national traitors who undermine the Southwest's unified anti-aggression actions. (6) Organize a foreign affairs support association, and immediately appoint preparatory members from each province, including: Sichuan (Li Boshen, Jin Fulan, Huang Shengxiang), Yunnan (Zhou Bogan, Gao Xuan, Yang Maozhang), Guizhou (Wang Xiaogong, Zhang Yunliang, Wei Xiangmo), Guangdong (Huang Linshu, Huo Guanghe, Li Renren), Guangxi (Wang Xunzhi, Liu Fan, Wang Gongdu), a total of fifteen people. An office was set up at the Asia Hotel on Changdi. After holding two preparatory meetings and telegraphing the authorities of each province to send responsible representatives to Guangzhou for a meeting, in addition to the representatives from Sichuan, Guizhou, Guangxi, and Guangdong, Long Yun from Yunnan Province also appointed Xiao Choumin, the president of the Hong Kong Fu Dian Bank, to come to Guangzhou to discuss everything with the local authorities. After the representatives of each province arrived in the province one after another, the Southwestern Foreign Affairs Association held an inaugural ceremony on the 22nd at the auditorium of the Provincial Party Department on Dadong Road. The opening ceremony was held at 1 p.m. in the afternoon, and more than 100 comrades from various provinces in Guangdong attended the meeting. Yang Maozhang, the representative of Yunnan, was elected as the chairman. Bai Chongxi attended the meeting and gave a speech, hoping for three points: (1) The association should publicize the situation of foreign oppression as much as possible to awaken the people to unite against foreign aggression. (2) Establish a Southwestern Bank so that the people of the Southwest and overseas Chinese who return to the country can have faith in it, so that they can invest and start industries with peace of mind. (3) Promote transportation in the Southwest. The roads in the Southwest should be connected first to facilitate transportation and connect the railways of the southwestern provinces to strengthen national defense. Then, Zhou Bogan and Du Zhiyuan from Yunnan reported on the current situation in Yunnan Province and the situation on the Yunnan border. Finally, Gao Xuan reported on the preparation process of the conference. After the report, discussions began and the following matters were resolved: (1) Approved the conference charter. (2) The conference declaration was handed over to the members for revision. (3) Submit to the Central Party Headquarters and the National Government and the First Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee, requesting the realization of the six principles set by the association. (4) Invite armed comrades from the southwestern provinces to become honorary members of the association. (5) Publish publications and organize branches in various provinces. (6) Raise funds, which will be collected by the executive and supervisory committee members from various provinces. (7) The executive and supervisory committee members will be elected by the preparatory committee members of each province and the members of the province. The results of the elections must be reported to the association within three days and will be ratified at the next general meeting. (8) It was decided to hold another meeting at 1 p.m. on the 27th. (23rd)

Shandong Library

Founding the Luoquanlou Han Painting Hall 64

▲Scheduled to Open on New Year's Day Next Year

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Provincial Library has made great efforts to collect ancient books and bronzes and stone inscriptions in recent years, and its collection is growing richer every day. Recently, it founded the Luoquanlou Han Painting Hall, which will be displayed in the original Hutianyijiao Building of the library. It is scheduled to open on New Year's Day of the 21st year (1932), and rubbings of the brick and tile inscriptions from the Shangtao Studio will be made for circulation. The details are as follows:

▲Inscriptions on Bricks and Tiles from the Shangtao Studio: The Gao family in Weixian, Shandong, has the most bricks and tiles from the Qin and Han dynasties. This summer, they sold them to the Japanese for 2,000 yuan. The Provincial Government Education Department learned of this and detained them in Qingdao. After several negotiations, they were transported to the Jinan Library for preservation. The inscriptions on bricks and tiles from the Shangtao Studio are original rubbings by Gao Hansheng. At that time, a total of four copies were made, and those who obtained them cherished them. According to the investigation, one of these four copies is now at Yanjing University. The paper is small and the rubbings are very rough and not complete. Xu Shichang and the Shandong Library each have a copy, and another copy is in Weixian, which is priced at 500 yuan. Wang Xiantang, the current director of the library, has made eight rubbings of the Qin and Han dynasty bricks and tiles obtained from the Gao family for circulation. All 600 types are in one copy, which is still named Inscriptions on Bricks and Tiles from the Shangtao Studio (it is said that the rubbings are 12 types more than Gao Hansheng's original version. 12 types, such as the Qin 12-character brick, were lost in Gao's original version and have been reconstructed).

▲Han Painting Hall: The painting hall has a large number of Han dynasty stone carvings, large and small, with a total of 50 pieces, of various styles. They are all inlaid on the walls. This spring, three particularly ancient tomb door stone carvings were transported from Weixian. The upper part is three goats, which means "Three Yangs Bring Prosperity". Below are two stones, carved into human figures, which are Shentu and Yulei. After being transported to the library, they were also inlaid on the walls, still in the shape of a tomb door. There is also a very good stone carving of the Emperor's chariot, but unfortunately it was purchased by the Germans. The library only has a rubbing, which is now hanging in the Han Painting Hall.

▲Luoquanlou: There are many spring collectors in Shandong, especially Chu Weiyuan of Laiyang, Ma Zhuwu of Licheng, Liu Yanting and Wang Jimen of Zhucheng, and Li Zhupeng of Lijin, all of whom have special books published. Among them, Ma's Hongou Huaxuan Spring Collection is exquisitely and extensively praised. Later, his manuscript writing board spring coins were taken away by his son-in-law Li. In the thirteenth year of Guangxu (1887), a book was printed with the remaining boards and circulated. After several changes in the world, they were scattered and lost. Last spring, Li's descendants donated 610 original carved boards of ancient springs and spring collections to the library, and 114 boards were obtained from the market, totaling 724 boards, 1,229 items, extensively collected and cited, forming a grand view. They are now displayed in the Hutianyijiao Building, renamed Luoquanlou, with the spring collections arranged on shelves according to their original categories, such as tools, coins, knife coins, and round laws. Their genealogy is listed separately, outlining the evolution, and the arrangement is clear. It is currently being arranged and is scheduled to open on New Year's Day next year for public exhibition.

Tao Ye Gong Proposes Conscription to Save the Country 65

Tao Ye Gong intends to submit a proposal for conscription to save the country at the National Crisis Conference and the National Salvation Conference in the near future. The main reasons are as follows: "Today, the foreign crisis is becoming increasingly urgent, and the people of the country are loudly calling for resistance to foreign aggression. All are paying attention to expanding military preparations. At the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee, Mr. He Xiangning and Mr. Wang Qi proposed the implementation of conscription, and the Guangdong Fourth Plenary Representatives Assembly also made the same proposal. I believe that China is in a desperate environment and everyone should achieve this goal. According to the results of China's past conscription, in the late Qing Dynasty, the 9th Division of the Jiangnan Army once implemented partial conscription. At that time, young people with lofty ideals and patriotic ideas enthusiastically responded to the call, and the seeds of revolution were also widely spread among the soldiers. The Xinhai Revolution was so easy to achieve because it was effective. When the European War broke out, Mr. Jiang Baili, the former principal of the Military Officer School, saw the intensity of the war and suggested to the Beijing government that it also advocate the implementation of conscription. He delineated two areas, Jingzhao and Heluo, as conscription pilot zones, and established a conscription training institute in Beijing, which was directly under the command of the office. Former middle and lower-level military officers were students, and they were taught special conscription subjects and the conscription systems of various countries. Three classes graduated successively, with several hundred people, who were assigned to various places as conscription commissioners. The effect was gradually evident. Unfortunately, the warlords of the Beiyang government wanted to maintain their private armed forces, like those who eat likin rice and do not want to cut likin taxes. Therefore, they came out to obstruct it in many ways, resulting in its interruption. If it could have continued at that time, then today there would have been a situation of all the people in the country being soldiers, and how could it be so vulnerable to a single battle? Moreover, the advantages and disadvantages of conscription and recruitment are obvious. To name a few of the major ones, no matter how large the number of standing troops under the recruitment system, it is ultimately limited. Once it fights against the enemy, there is no replenishment, how can it continue? Under the conscription system, the number of orderly discharged veterans increases with age, and there is no need to worry about the lack of replenishment of troops. This is one. The recruitment system is mercenary in nature. Recruits are motivated by money, and are either unemployed hooligans or long-term bandits in the camp. Therefore, in the past, China had the saying "Good men do not become soldiers". With this kind of person carrying weapons, how can one hope that they will not disturb the people? Those who are conscripted under the conscription system are all educated, have a clean family background, and are employed. With good quality, they will be able to inspire the spirit of sacrificing themselves to save the country, in order to achieve decisive victory. This is two. The recruitment system takes money as a prerequisite. In today's China, when the people are poor and the finances are exhausted, huge amounts of military pay must still be spent to support useless soldiers. If this continues, all policies will be abandoned and the country will be bankrupt in the end. The conscription system is completely obligatory in nature. The state does not provide military pay to soldiers, except for providing food and clothing. Therefore, huge amounts of money can be saved to ease the country's financial resources. This is three. The warlords can recruit troops at any time and anywhere to expand the strength of their private armies under the recruitment system. The conscription system has certain laws and procedures to restrict it, and soldiers also have a considerable understanding and will not be used by them. Then the warlords will not rely on it, and internal wars can be avoided. This is four. Today, although China is oppressed by the unequal treaties of the imperialists, it is not as restricted by the Treaty of Versailles as Germany and Austria, which restricts its military preparations. Therefore, it is necessary to rise up in time and defend ourselves with force. It is imperative to implement conscription. I hope that a unified government will be established, a national defense plan will be determined, and a conscription order will be promulgated at the same time. A conscription committee will be established in the central government to actively prepare and implement the conscription plan in the shortest possible time, so that it can fight against the enemy and secure our humiliation.

Page 17

Important News Two

The Fall of Huang'an 66

▲ Zhao Guanying's Fate Unknown

Hankou Dispatch: The 69th Division, trapped in Huang'an, was overcome by the bandits on the night of the 22nd of this month (December) after running out of ammunition and food, and failing to receive reinforcements. The county town was breached with heavy casualties. Division Commander Zhao Guanying fought bravely and was seriously wounded; his fate is unknown. In the two years since the Red Bandits have been seizing cities and territories, there has been none as rampant as this time. Huang'an is located in eastern Hubei, bordering Anhui Province to the north, connected to Macheng in the east, Huangpi in the west, and bordering Huanggang to the south. It is the most culturally developed area of Hubei Province. When the Revolutionary Army arrived in Wuhan in 1926, their party manipulated from within, secretly planting forces. The counties in eastern Hubei were especially cultivated, and the banditry in the corner of Huang'an was even more severe. Later, after the separation of the Kuomintang and the Communist Party, followed by the Guizhou clique's "purification of the countryside," many were killed with broadswords and axes. However, the Red Bandits of Huang'an still held their mountainous terrain and resisted the enemy with all their might. Except for the county town, the rest was within their sphere of influence, and the government troops could do nothing about it. The Huang'an County Magistrate could only sit and guard the empty city, issuing orders that only extended five miles. Later, Xia Douyin, as commander of the 13th Division, concurrently served as the Hubei Provincial Garrison Commander and engaged in purification and suppression. Xia was from Macheng, Hubei, and many of his officers and soldiers were from Huang'an and Macheng, making them extremely familiar with the terrain. After encircling and suppressing for some time, the banditry was slightly curbed. However, the areas of Qiliping, Taohuadian, Hekou, and Shanting in the county still could not avoid being the bandits' lair. This year, Li Mingzhong was appointed as the Pacification Supervisor of the Henan-Anhui-Hubei Border Area, and Huang'an was within his defense area. He once used several divisions of troops to conquer the bandit nest of Qiliping, and the bandits fled to the border areas of Henan and Anhui, allowing the area to be slightly at peace. At that time, the garrison in Huang'an was Zhao Guanying's 69th Division and Li Dingwu's New Third Brigade. Unexpectedly, two months ago, Li's unit suddenly received orders to move to Echeng, and Zhao's unit also received orders to move elsewhere. Li's unit moved first, and Zhao temporarily stayed to deter the area because the 33rd Division that was supposed to take over had not arrived. With a single force, the bandits took the opportunity to steal and attack. Zhao's unit was reorganized from the Henan Army, totaling about five or six thousand people. Their equipment and ammunition were not very sufficient, and their food and pay were extremely strained. It was a great struggle for them to resist fierce bandits such as Kuang Jizhu and Xu Jishen, so they held on to the Huang'an County town to await reinforcements. At that time, the Red Bandits attacked the city with all their strength, and at the same time mobilized other units to gather at Taohua Hekou, blocking transportation. Zhao's unit's supplies could not be transported, and reinforcements could not arrive immediately. Zhao himself has always been known for his bravery and skill in battle, and fought fiercely with the bandits more than twenty times, all without success. Deputy Division Commander Wang Yiqun rushed to Wuhan, tearfully begging for troops. On the 22nd of this month, the bandits increased their troops to attack the city, and the city was breached the next morning. Zhao fought bravely and was seriously wounded; his fate is unknown. What is rumored on the roads is that he has already been killed. The deaths of the people and the loss of property are even more uncountable. It is truly a great disaster. Deputy Division Commander Wang Yiqun, after hearing the news in Hankou, immediately rushed to Huangpi to collect the remnants of the troops nearby, and telegraphed the Hubei Pacification Commissioner's Office, requesting condolences for the dead and wounded officers and soldiers, to commend the loyal and brave. The original telegram is as follows: "Hankou Resident Hubei Pacification Commissioner's Office Director He Junjian, Huang'an is located in a remote border area, with dense mountains and forests. As early as 1927, it fell into the bandit area. The army turns pale at the mention of it, regarding it as a dangerous path. This division was ordered to advance and suppress, and immediately advanced in the rain, breaking through the enemy at Ta'ergang, Jiashanzhai, and Fengxiuyi, and was finally able to arrive. After taking over the defense for five months, there was not a day without fighting, and every battle was fierce. Until mid-October, Taohua, a natural barrier, was blocked and the 33rd Division did not come. Hekou, a strategic point, the Provisional Third Brigade left without defense, delaying the deadline. Transportation was blocked, the dangerous city was isolated, and the lone army struggled, holding on for three months. The ground was frozen and the sky was cold, and people were still wearing summer clothes, trapped in a heavy siege, without food or ammunition. Still, they tempered the morale of the troops, encouraging each other with public loyalty, embracing the determination to perish with the city, and the courage to achieve benevolence and take righteousness. Knowing that weak wood cannot bear a heavy burden, and its strength will inevitably break, but after receiving the order, they did not dare to consider the gains and losses. In the last month, there were more than twenty battles, with countless dead and wounded, and moans filling the city. On December, the day of nourishment, the reinforcements failed, and the bandits attacked even more fiercely with all their strength. At this time, there was no grain left in the city, and the doors of the people were burned. They fought with white blades, and flesh and blood flew everywhere. They killed the enemy with empty stomachs, and moaned to their death. The tragic situation cannot be described in words. The disparity between the crowd and the few, and the different situations of the host and the guest, were different. The city was breached at dawn, and Division Commander Zhao fought bravely and was seriously wounded; his fate is unknown. Only a thousand or so people escaped. Most of the rest are missing. I am at Wulidun, five miles north of Huangpi City, collecting and reorganizing them. In recent days, about three thousand scattered officers and soldiers have gathered. After slightly reorganizing them, I will ask for plans to complete the unfinished work of Division Commander Zhao and avenge the defeat of all the officers and soldiers. Knowing that the army has been defeated and the city has been lost, I am filled with shame and embarrassment. Although I have done my best, my heart still feels uneasy. I hope that Your Excellency will reward the hearts of the people and encourage the future, and give some comfort to the living and give condolences to the dead and wounded. I am collecting the troops and waiting for orders in Huangpi. I respectfully telegraph and ask, and respectfully await your instructions. Deputy Division Commander Wang Yizhao of the 69th Division of the Army respectfully kowtows, (December 30th)"

The Course of Gan Bandits' Intrusion and Capture of Wuyuan 67

Wuyuan Dispatch: Since the tense situation, the Red Bandits of Jiangxi Province have become increasingly rampant. Fang Zhimin, Shao Shiping, Zhou Jianping and other groups in northeastern Jiangxi have also taken the opportunity to move, hoping to revive. Last month, the main force of Fang and Shao were attacked by the 9th Division of Jiang Dingwen and Lu Xiaochen's division in Geyuan, Beiban, Yiyang, and the Ninth District of Guangxin. Although they were defeated, their strength was not greatly damaged. Recently, the troops of Fang and Shao's 10th Army, the First and Second Regiments, Tang Zaigang, and others, are also rushing to advance to northern Jiangxi, coveting the border between Anhui and Zhejiang, and seeking a new base. For a month, the troops have been galloping left and right in the intermediate counties of Jiangxi, Anhui, and Zhejiang, engaging in large-scale activities. Although their goal is to take Zhejiang and neglect Anhui, the counties on the Zhejiang border, such as Kaihua, Jiangshan, and Changshan, have security teams and defense forces stationed there, which are easy to dispatch. If the bandit army enters, they can be resisted immediately. Moreover, places such as Huabu in Kaihua have been occupied by the bandits taking advantage of the gaps, and they have plundered wealth, fulfilling their wishes. Only the territory of Anhui is coveted. Wuyuan is the first important gateway in southern Anhui, bordering Dexing, with weak defense forces, but with a false reputation for wealth. Fang and others have coveted it for a long time. This time, they suddenly attacked Wuyuan City. It is heard that they had previously scouted that the city's defense garrison had been withdrawn and the local self-defense force was unable to resist. On the 16th of this month, Tang Zaigang, Zhou Jianping, and others led their Red Army and spearmen teams, totaling more than 2,000 people, and attacked Badu, Xinjian, Haikou, and Wuyuan City in Dexing at the same time. Zhou led a part to attack Dexing, and Tang led a part to attack Wuyuan, both at the same time, in order to connect the two places. It happened that the Wuyuan County Magistrate, Qi Feini, had left his post to go to the province a week ago. The city defense police team, due to the border situation being quiet for days and the alarm of attacking the city becoming a common word, did not suspect any accidents, and their defenses were lax. On the day before the bandits attacked the city, some of the bandit army had already disguised themselves and sneaked into the county town, planting willows between the city's moats as a pre-arranged internal response. At four o'clock in the morning on the 17th, Tang led his troops straight from Tongbu to the outside of the West Gate of Wuyuan City, occupying Lion Mountain outside the city. (This mountain is high and steep, and the entire city can be seen clearly.) (First, they sent a commando team of more than a hundred people, holding wooden ladders to climb the city wall, recognizing the willows and firing guns. The lurking plainclothes team in the city also fired guns in response. The guards and squad leaders at the West Gate heard the alarm and got up to escape, but were shot and killed in bed by the lurking bandits. The Northwest and South gates were also opened at the same time, and the bandits occupying Lion Mountain immediately fired horns and drove into the city in detachments. Suddenly, gunshots rang out everywhere, and bullets were like a string of pearls. At this time, all the residents in the city were still dreaming. When they heard the gunshots and woke up in shock, it was too late to escape. Order was immediately thrown into a chaotic state. After the bandit army entered the city, Tang's bandit headquarters occupied the Mei Hua Li kerosene warehouse in the west of the city. The rest of the detachments surrounded the agencies, and those who suffered looting were the County Higher Primary School. When the school's sounding bell rang, the bandit army took it as a warning. A group of dozens of Red Bandits rushed straight into the school, destroying the equipment at will. The students' suitcases and bedding were all moved out, and the school director, Cheng, teacher Wang Shaotang, and three students were arrested and interrogated at the bandit headquarters. At the same time, the County Government and the Police Division, and the Self-Defense Corps of the First District, were all surrounded. Fortunately, most of the police team got up early to prepare and quickly escaped through the back door, firing guns to cover their escape. Both sides fought in the streets. A part of them scattered, and a part of them escaped through the East Gate. The Self-Defense Corps, because the Ziyang Academy where they were stationed had a better terrain, led the members of the corps by Corps Leader Zhan Yunxing to fight desperately, killing four Red Bandits, and leaving the city from the North Gate. Later, they encountered a bandit army and fought fiercely for an hour. Because the crowd was outnumbered, they retreated to Wukou in the northern countryside. As for the bandit army besieging the County Government, they searched for the weapons of the guards in the government, and arrested Section Chief Yu of the Second Section. They also divided into groups to search the Daya Warehouse and food warehouse, and released the prisoners from the prison. Then they used umbrella clothes to set fire, burning everywhere, reaching the front door of the County Government. The poor people, men and women, who lived next door, fearing that their houses would be affected, knelt down and begged not to destroy them, and were spared. The rest of the flower hall, inner rooms, prisons, granaries, etc., were all set on fire, turning them into empty rubble. The church north of the city was also affected. The priest of the church, because he couldn't hide in time, was taken away by the bandits. Other shops and wealthy residents were all entered and searched by them. After this thorough search, the walls of the streets and alleys were covered with slogans and announcements, signed with the names of Tang Zaigang, Chairman of the Jiangxi Northeastern Provincial Committee, etc., in the Gregorian calendar 1931. The bandits also ordered shops and residents not to close their doors, otherwise they would be burned and the residents would be shot. Therefore, the shops and residents all had their doors wide open. More than 500 spearmen outside the West Gate, each holding wooden and bamboo sticks, divided into groups to move cloth, silk, foreign goods, bedding, clothes, salt, oil, food, groceries, etc., from the merchants in the Chengjia Street area of the West Gate. For a time, boxes and bags were piled up, accumulated in the riverbeds, and hired boats to load them, just like unloading cargo at a port. When the bandit army went to the store to buy things, they gave the value with current silver and copper coins, or with their own poor people's securities. The shop assistants had to accept them obediently and dare not refuse to use them. On this day, all the bandit army and more than a thousand spearmen searched the city from six in the morning to eight in the evening. The merchants' possessions were looted. At about nine o'clock in the evening, the bandits suddenly ordered the team to line up and camp at Lion Mountain outside the city, leaving only dozens of staff bandits stationed in the Chamber of Commerce, demanding 150,000 yuan, otherwise they would burn it down without pardon. At this time, the chairman and standing committee members of the Chamber of Commerce had already fled. Finally, several shop assistants represented and maintained it, repeatedly begging the bandits to reduce it, and they agreed to pay 50,000 yuan in cash. In order to avoid the suffering of the whole city, the representatives tried their best to raise money from all sides, but only got 7,000 yuan. They reported to the bandit leader that it was difficult to raise money, and it was impossible to meet the number of 50,000, and they agreed to reduce it to 10,000 yuan. The representatives also went to different places to dig, deeply suffering that they could not find a wealthy one, and there was no way to raise money. It was already noon at night, and the bandits urged them very urgently. They had to hand over the 8,000 yuan that they had collected. At this time, the bandit leader could no longer wait, and actually detained Wang Huayin, a partner of the Qian Yuan Pharmacy, and instructed him to quickly prepare 2,000 yuan to redeem him. Then he ordered all of them to withdraw from the county seat, lined up and set off, and also took away the Catholic Church priest, Wang Shaotang, and Section Chief Yu of the county government, and other six people. The looted property, the important ones were carried by the spearmen, and the secondary goods were loaded by boat, divided into water and land escorts, and retreated to the Dexing border along the original road. On the morning of the 18th, there was no trace of the bandit army in Wuyuan City, but no one was in charge of security, and the situation was still chaotic. It is estimated that the number of Red Bandits who attacked Wuyuan this time, including the spearmen, was about 1,600 to 700 people, of which one-third had guns, half of which were unarmed fake weapons, and bullets were also scarce. The losses inside and outside the city were the heaviest in the Chengjia Street area of the West Gate. The East and South gates were less damaged because they were remote. Among them, the biggest losses, in addition to the County Higher Primary School, were Jichang Pawnshop, Lishun Cloth Shop, Zhongde Xile Foreign Goods Shop, Meihua Li Kerosene Warehouse, Hexingxiang Grocery Shop, Ruisheng Cloth Shop, and wealthy households Jin Xinpu, Hu Quanchen, Sun Qintang, etc., more than a hundred families. Other losses of one or two hundred yuan are countless. Among the residents who were shot and killed, there was a woman in the north of the city, a tailor, a pedestrian, and four policemen. The loss of firearms was about thirty. It was a huge disaster in Wuyuan since the Hong Yang Rebellion. At this moment, the parties in the city and countryside have gathered to discuss and plan to handle the aftermath. The police team and self-defense corps who fled to the countryside have also returned to the city yesterday to take charge of security. Division Commander Ruan of the 55th Division stationed in Leping, after receiving the telephone call from the Jingdezhen Chamber of Commerce and the request for assistance from Wuyuan, agreed to send Zhang Brigade stationed in Dexing to lead the Wu and Wang regiments to Wuyuan to defend and suppress the bandits. It is heard that the Han battalion can arrive in the county seat first today. Now, the people's hearts have gradually stabilized, (December 22nd).

Local Communications

Wuxi 69

The kidnapped hostages of Xin'an Town are rescued. Yao Qibao, a partner of Shuntai South Goods Store, and Wang Jian'san, the owner of Xinchang Rice Store, in Xin'an Town, the 13th District, were kidnapped by more than 20 bandits from the Great Lake on the 30th of last month, and have not yet escaped. Recently, the bandits instructed a bandit to disguise himself as a beggar and contact Wang Jian'san's family. As a result, he was redeemed for 200 yuan and arrived home safely yesterday. As for Yao Qibao, he is still imprisoned in the bandit's lair because he has no money to redeem him.

The bandit sent a letter to scare a rural woman to death. Chen Peiquan, a villager in Chenjia Lane, Qianshan, about three miles north of Zhangjing Bridge, in the 7th District (Huai Market), was over fifty years old, had a well-to-do family, and had dozens of acres of good land, which was coveted by bandits. In the last ten days of last month, he suddenly received a threatening letter from the bandits, demanding 400 yuan in foreign money. In the first ten days of this month, he continued to receive a letter, demanding 700 yuan in foreign money. After receiving the letter, Chen was extremely frightened and did not dare to stay at home. Chen's wife, Zhu, suffered a heavy shock and suddenly became ill, bleeding from her nostrils, spitting green water, and unable to eat or drink. She was treated by Chinese and Western doctors, but her illness was severe and the medicine was ineffective, and she died a tragic death the day before yesterday.

Jiangyin 70

Searching for opium to be sent to the province for verification. Jiangyin is located at an important port on the Yangtze River and was originally known as the opium wharf. The day before yesterday (25th) late at night, passengers Wei Jincheng, Long Bangsui, Hu Yimin, and Hu Peize of a passenger ship took a small boat in the Taixing port area, claiming to be the directors of the fortress inspection. (According to Wei Dacheng, Chun Yan once served as the director of the fortress and the joint defense office, and has now been relieved of his post.) They planned to board the Taikoo Company's Wuhu ship to search for opium. Later, they were stopped by a British warship, and the four of Wei Dacheng were detained on the ship for four days and taken to Shanghai to be questioned by the British consul. On the 29th, Deputy Consul Jitesen took the four on the British warship Kricto and arrived in the province in the afternoon, handing them over to the provincial government for verification.

The principal's rape of a female student case is sentenced. Qian Nanyun, the principal of the Qingyang Temple Primary School, was detained after being investigated and clarified by the county for the case of raping Liu Xiufeng, a 12-year-old female student. Yesterday (30th), the county submitted the sentence: Qian Nanyun was sentenced to nine years and four months for rape, and six months for fleeing in fear of crime, to be executed together for nine years and five months.

Zhenjiang 71

The Nanjing middle school students have been resolved. The Nanjing middle school students have repeatedly come to the province to petition because they opposed Principal Zhang Tong, but no results have been obtained. Yesterday afternoon, more than 300 people arrived again and went to the Education Department. The Provincial Committee Li Mingyang received them and argued for a long time. Li commissioned the Provincial Committee and Chairman Gu to decide to send Yang Naikang, the chief of the First Section of the Education Department, to the school to maintain school affairs before the new Director of the Education Department took over. Xiang Zhishu, the chief of general affairs, maintained the food. After the new Director of the Education Department took over, the provincial government will formally commission the principal after a meeting. The students were satisfied, but they had to return to school with Yang Jun. It is planned to start tonight. It is also heard that the new Director of the Education Department can also come to the province in the next few days.

Zhenguan tea house clerk absconds with huge sum of money. Cheng Jiyun, a clerk at the Zhenjiang Customs, ordered the tea house clerk Guo Degui to take 1,000 yuan in silver to the Bank of China by the river at two o'clock yesterday afternoon. Unexpectedly, Guo absconded with the money. He immediately reported to the Fifth Branch, and the family members of Guo were summoned to hand over Guo to be punished.

Retired soldiers organize the National Salvation Army. Xie Guangzi, Zou Zigang and other eleven retired soldiers, in view of the rampant Japanese violence and the danger of Jinzhou, specifically initiated the organization of the Jiangsu Retired Soldiers Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Army. The preparatory office is located in the Zhenjiang Fukang Hotel. It has been reported to the Public Security Bureau for record. Once approved, it will actively proceed and be established as soon as possible.

The salaries of teachers and staff will continue to be inquired about. All the teachers and staff of the county previously demanded salaries from the county government. The date of distribution, 3. How to allocate it. According to the answer, about 800 yuan, at most 1,000 yuan, will be distributed before the 30th.

Ningbo 74

Reporting that the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce used the National Salvation Fund. Lin Qinxiang, the former chairman of the Ningbo General Chamber of Commerce, is suspected of using the 40,000 yuan of the National Salvation Fund by taking advantage of his position for personal gain. Jin Zhenxiang, the supervisory committee of the chamber, reported in writing. The Chamber of Commerce believed that the matter was of great importance, so it convened a temporary executive meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss the results. Because the case involved the affairs of the former General Chamber of Commerce, four members, Zhou Taozhuo, Dianying, Lu Benlu, and Mao Jieying, were first recommended to review the accounts before further deliberation. Furthermore, Lin Jianzhong, the standing committee member of the Yin County Party Department, and Chen Baolin, the county magistrate, consulted yesterday afternoon on the case of Lin Qinxiang, the original custodian of the Chamber of Commerce, delaying the payment of the National Salvation Fund. As a result, 1. Reply to Lin Qinxiang, the original custodian of the Chamber of Commerce, to hand over the principal and interest of the National Salvation Fund in custody in full before January 20, 1932. As for the 45,000 yuan in financial bonds of the guarantee, since it is not a substitute for cash, it is difficult to recognize it as sufficient guarantee, and other reliable guarantee should be provided within five days of receiving the document. 2. Since Lin Qinxiang is the original custodian of the Chamber of Commerce, the Chamber of Commerce should be ordered to take responsibility for handling the report and verification as soon as possible.

Anqing 75

Anhui-Xun Line Ping An Ferry Boat Accident. The Taichang Company's Ping An Ferry Boat, which operates on the Anhui-Xun line, left Anhui for Xun at 8:00 am on the 28th. When it was more than ten miles upstream of Yangjiatao, Anqing, a tragedy occurred due to a boiler explosion. The ferry boat had been suspended for one day due to rain, and the passengers were particularly crowded that morning. When it opened to Yangjiatao, the boiler suddenly exploded, and the machinery was destroyed, resulting in more than a hundred passengers who were warming themselves by the furnace and cabin passengers near the boiler, as well as employees serving in the engine room, being injured and killed. Another part of the people, because the incident happened suddenly, panicked and threw themselves into the river, and the number of those who were buried in the fish was also unknown. Fortunately, the Anfeng patrol ship was patrolling the river and passed by the place, rescuing many lives and towing the ship to Anhui, mooring on the Jiang'an outside the West Gate. For a time, no less than 10,000 people went to visit, helping the old and the young. Then the Martial Law Command and the Provincial Public Security Bureau sent teams to the village to send the injured to the Tongren Boai and Boji hospitals for treatment according to their severity. The dead were claimed by their families, and the rest were lying on the shore, bloody and unrecognizable, which was unbearable to see. Now the company has reported to the official officials to handle the aftermath and telegraphed to the Xun General Office to ask for everything.

Nanjing Middle School Students Petitioned in Province Due to Food Shortage 76

Since former Principal Zhang Tong resigned from Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing Middle School, Lin Geng, who is responsible for maintaining school affairs, has been quite dissatisfied with all the measures. The students have sent representatives to the province four times to petition, but due to the fact that the new Director of Education has not yet come to the province to take office, there have been no satisfactory results. Recently, there have been problems with the meals. Yao Yuanzhu, the secretary of the Education Department, and Han Shoujin, the chief of the General Affairs Section, personally advised the cooks to continue cooking as usual, and the Education Department was responsible for the expenses. Unexpectedly, the two cooks of the senior and junior high school suddenly left the school the night before (29th), and all the students had no food, which caused great panic. More than 200 people gathered and came to the province by car from Beijing at 9 am yesterday (30th), heading to the Education Department to make the fifth petition. The Education Department reported the situation to the provincial government, and the provincial government recommended Committee Member Mingyang and Secretary Jin to go to the Education Department to comfort and persuade the students, and stated that the Education Department would send personnel to Beijing that night to recall the cooks and take care of the students' meals at school. Regarding the selection of the acting principal, it will be discussed with Chairman Gu and appointed. The students were satisfied and dispersed. The provincial government ordered Yang Naikang, the chief of the Second Section of the Education Department, to quickly go to Beijing to be responsible for temporarily maintaining school affairs. In addition, the Education Department appointed two staff members, Xiang Zhishu and Liu Yuhe, to go to Beijing first to solve the food problem. As for the candidate for the new principal, it will be decided after the new Director Zhou takes office.

Not Removing Garden Weeds Zhai Fu Talks

Three Questions and Three Answers for the New Year (Part 1) 103

Not Removing Garden Zhai Talks Weeds (Once upon a time, a king took three questions to ask a hermit, saying: "Who is the most important person? What is the most important thing? What is the most important word?")

If China's 400 million Adou wanted to ask me these three questions, I would not hesitate to answer:

Young people are the most important people; cherishing young people is the most important thing; speaking justly for young people is the most important word.

In recent years, young people have been chopped down like radish heads, basket after basket. The chopped heads can be used to build a mountain, and several great men sit on the mountain, drinking and bowing. I now inform His Majesty Adou that from now on, the government must not be allowed to kill people, especially young people.

1. Killing cannot stop killing. "Killing to stop killing" is a superstition. Those in power always believe "killing one as a warning to a hundred." This is no different from the imperialists' mantra of "war to stop war." In reality, war invites war, and killing invites killing. Generally, there are two types of people the government wants to kill: one is bandits forced by hunger and cold; the other is political enemies with different beliefs. Bandits cannot be stopped by killing; bandits will stop when hunger and cold are stopped. Political enemies see being killed as achieving benevolence and dying as martyrdom. Killing them is like pouring soup to stop boiling water. As the ancients said well, "If the people do not fear death, why use death to frighten them?"

2. Killing is the behavior of a madman. A person with hatred in their heart, like a madman or a lunatic, will kill. "Politics is righteousness." The government should not have hatred, so how can it kill?

3. Killers are unkind. Mr. Sun Yat-sen encouraged people to practice loyalty, filial piety, integrity, righteousness, benevolence, love, and peace. Benevolence and love mean not liking to kill people. Killing people with people is the worst kind of unkindness.

4. Killers are unwise. The French Revolution could not tolerate the scientist Lavoisier, which was unwise of the French people. Who can guarantee that among the countless young people killed in China in recent years, there are not a few talents like Lavoisier? To put it another way, the cost of raising a very ordinary person from childhood to the age of twenty is at least two to three thousand yuan. Now someone throws three thousand or two thousand silver dollars into the sea, can that be considered intelligent? Those who have the ability to tame a tiger always want to catch a live tiger, because a live tiger is much more useful than a dead tiger. Only clumsy hunters kill tigers. Tigers should not be killed, let alone people? We should know that if the killing intent does not stop, it will inevitably lead to mutual killing. In the end, it is just using someone else's knife to kill your own people.

5. Killers are not brave. Killing does not stem from hatred but must stem from fear. The government should not have hatred, let alone fear. How many lives are buried in this irrational fear!

6. Mr. Sun Yat-sen wrote a couplet: "Cultivate the righteous spirit of heaven and earth; emulate the perfect people of ancient and modern times." The righteous spirit of heaven and earth is the virtue of loving life. None of the perfect people of ancient and modern times did not embody the virtue of loving life, and none of them approved of killing people. Confucius said of Emperor Yao: "Only Heaven is great, only the Emperor emulates it." Because what he practiced was the way of Heaven, the way of kings. Yao was a perfect person in China. As for Shun's exile of Gonggong, release of Huan Dou, killing of the Sanmiao, and execution of Gun, he was far inferior to Yao. Ancient perfect people abroad, such as Sakyamuni and Jesus Christ, all forbade killing. "Cultivate the righteous spirit of heaven and earth; emulate the perfect people of ancient and modern times" cannot be achieved with empty words; it must be issued as a political order, starting with the abolition of the death penalty.

7. Specific measures for abolishing the death penalty are listed below:

A. All capital crimes shall be changed to life imprisonment;

B. Find an island by the sea that can accommodate hundreds of thousands of people to cultivate and work as a place to educate and rehabilitate these prisoners;

C. Establish large-scale science museums, libraries, farms, forests, handicraft factories, and mechanical factories on the island for various prisoners to study and learn skills;

D. Establish other life-necessary institutions on the island for prisoners to regulate their lives;

E. The entire island shall have one chief supervisor appointed by the government;

F. The entire island shall have an unlimited number of supervisors appointed by the chief supervisor, or selected from among the prisoners who have appropriate qualifications;

G. Prisoners who make scientific discoveries or create inventions in their work may regain their freedom.

Please Start from New Year's Day 104

— Ding Ming

Friends. Today is New Year's Day. Think of the suffering of the people, the many difficulties of the nation. If you compare it to this day last year, how much more sorrow it brings. In this brand-new New Year, who doesn't feel a sense of imperfection? However, today, at the starting point filled with vitality, I hope everyone will engrave the following points in their hearts and never forget them. I also sincerely pray that everyone, especially young men and women, will "do" them practically. Only then will it be good.

1. Starting from New Year's Day, get up every morning before dawn and exercise the body for thirty minutes to invigorate the blood circulation throughout the body, making it as strong as steel, in preparation for going to the front lines to defend against insults and share the national crisis.

2. Starting from New Year's Day, continue to read books and newspapers that are beneficial to body and mind for at least one hundred and twenty minutes (add one time allowance including breaks).

3. Starting from New Year's Day, practice a simple life, saving on clothing and food, living in peace, getting used to labor, cultivating a full spirit, and demonstrating a loyal and responsible attitude.

4. Starting from New Year's Day, everyone should automatically eliminate all vanity consumption, such as drinking, smoking, gambling, decorations, etc., and develop a personality free of bad habits. Furthermore, donate the money saved to national salvation funds or other public welfare funds.

5. Starting from New Year's Day, everyone should expand publicity and penetrate into the people, so that every Chinese person does not use a single cent of enemy goods and clenches their teeth to use less of the foreign goods that economically invade us. On the one hand, strive to find ways to produce, improve and manufacture our country's original materials, and transport them to various countries to recover our previous losses.

6. Starting from New Year's Day, have a righteous and bright mind and a concept of serving society and putting public interests before private ones. Based on human love and mutual assistance, unite sincerely to correct the reality of social morals.

7. Starting from New Year's Day, the inherent courage, spirit, and heroic demeanor of every young person should be promoted and magnified as a whole.

Get up, get up. "The plan for the year lies in spring, and the plan for the day lies in the morning." These words are so true. Get up, get up, countrymen, dear young men and women. Please start from New Year's Day.

A Few Words on the Twenty-First Year of the Republic 106

— Song Lu

Another year has easily passed. It's New Year's Day again. The Republic of China was founded, and now it's the twenty-first year. I will now share some superficial views for conversational aid.

Our country has suffered many humiliations at the hands of the Japanese, but the Twenty-One Demands are the most severe. Now, as the twenty-first year arrives, I hope that the people of the country will firmly remember the Twenty-One Demands and work hard to resist Japan in order to wash away this humiliation. So that after twenty-one years, there will be no more Twenty-One Demands. Countrymen! Twenty-one, twenty-one! Startling and terrifying. Washing away humiliation and striving for strength depends on this year. Twenty-one is the beginning of the character "共" (gong, meaning "common" or "communist"). This year, be careful to prevent the communist party's slight movements. Fortunately, below "共" is "八" (ba, meaning "eight"), which is a symbol of separation. Perhaps within the communist party, during the twenty-first year, they will voluntarily separate and collapse.

Chiang Kai-shek held power for the longest time, but he stepped down and left in the winter of the twentieth year. Some say that the character "蔣" (Jiang) begins with "廿" (nian, meaning "twenty"), so he could not continue to the twenty-first year.

Someone might ask, "What sign does General Ma Zhanshan, who fights against Japan with his lone army, have in the twenty-first year?" I say, how can it be said there is none? The character "馬" (Ma, meaning "horse") in the rhyme category clearly indicates twenty-one. Therefore, the horse of the twenty-first year must become a pillar of the country. Some people heard this and clapped their hands and laughed.

▲ Errata: In the previous day's "Idle Chats from the Weed-Free Studio" in Shen Bao's "Poetry School," A, "用" (yong, to use) was mistakenly written as "因" (yin, because) in the discussion of using corners for business. B, "間" (jian, between) was mistakenly written as "問" (wen, to ask) in "無間他我汝" (no gap between him, me, you). C, "示" (shi, to show) was mistakenly written as "亦" (yi, also) in "示别於奴工畜工" (distinguishing between slave labor and livestock labor). Also, in "Respectfully Presented to National Teachers," "熊掌與魚不可兼" (one cannot have both bear paws and fish), "與魚" (with fish) was mistakenly written as "魚義" (fish meaning).

The Story of Two Soldiers' Buildings 107

— Owner of the Seeking Happiness Studio

▲ Prologue

Recently, I wrote a long episodic novel for Shen Bao called "The Story of Two Soldiers' Buildings." At first glance, the name seems to be a cliché of legendary descriptions of talented scholars and beautiful women. But the story in this book is not like that when written by my clumsy pen. What I want to write is a whole story with ingenious structure. And the nature of the story is perfectly in line with ordinary modernity. Although the title is only about "The Story of Two Soldiers' Buildings," it is not a beautiful and splendid marriage. The two protagonists, a man and a woman, are neither a heroic warrior-scholar nor a female hero like a general. However, their marriage was formed during the military period. When this period passed, all their hopes disappeared like bubbles, and their marriage came to an end. The general plot is about a top university student who is dissatisfied with the marriage arranged for him by his family. He has two other lovers outside, one is a female student, and the other is a famous prostitute who has married a wealthy man. Later, because his hometown suffered from bandit disasters, his parents died, and all his assets were lost. The famous prostitute could provide him with money and find a way out for him. So he abandoned his love and betrayed the female student, resolutely marrying the famous prostitute. Finally, with the power of the famous prostitute, he obtained a clue from the concubine of a certain military governor and was drawn into becoming a military officer. He also appeased and incorporated the bandits who had killed his parents into the army. The famous prostitute was also complacent and became a very prominent military officer's wife. In this process, the female student who lost her love, whose father was originally a greedy county magistrate, was accused of dereliction of duty due to a case, and her situation became very bad. She joined the army hospital as a nurse and fell in love with a lame doctor. Unexpectedly, the doctor had another most sad love story and could not accept her love, which made her feel very resentful. However, this unfaithful man, after his success, brought his only surviving weak younger brother by his side and sent him to the model youth army to enlist. Who knew that this ignorant child often hung out with his sister-in-law and the military governor's concubines, causing a bit of ambiguous suspicion and suffering a major blow. When he personally sent this dying younger brother to the hospital, he unintentionally met the female student again. However, she looked down on him even more. Because of the misfortune of his deceased younger brother, he was very afraid of losing his official position and tried his best to please a certain military governor again, seeking out the most beautiful street performer to be sent to the military governor as a concubine. But that girl also had another lover and used a passive resistance to move the generous heart of a certain military governor, who released her and sent her away with money. However, he was still promoted to the commander of the guard brigade, and everything went smoothly. He continued to be a good official. Several years later, the military governor was defeated and fled in despair. The street performer and her lover worked as boatmen and rescued the military governor from the encirclement out of gratitude for their previous kindness. At the same time, he also lost his job and resigned, hiding in the concession. When he was an official, both husband and wife spent lavishly and did not save much money. After some time, the military governor was unlikely to rise again, and they became extremely poor. The famous prostitute recalled the past, like a strange dream. Once she woke up, she deeply felt that staying together like this was harmful and useless to him. She advocated going their separate ways and looking for a way to make a living. She also advised him to return to his hometown to salvage the remnants of his life and die as a reformed person returning to his roots. He bid farewell to the famous prostitute, first found the female student, and was rejected by her. He had no choice but to go home and marry the country girl who was still his fiancée, and lived out his days as a farmer. As for the famous prostitute, her whereabouts are not very clear. Some say she was having an affair with an old man who ran an opium den, and others saw her working as a female receptionist in a barber shop. Gradually, it became impossible to verify. Such a story, with many complex aspects, is written into a twenty-episode episodic novel. It describes love, war, martial arts, and various societies and characters. Naturally, it must be described very faithfully and meticulously to show the life of this era and its cycle of cause and effect. But what I hold is an objective attitude. In addition to describing it very faithfully and meticulously for disclosure and exhibition, so that the general readers can get a little hint or association, there is no subjective meaning of praising or criticizing any aspect or satirizing any character. From the past warlords to these confused men and women, I think they are all victims of the times. They and she are all very pitiful. As for this description in this article, it can be said to be a prologue or an explanation. It has nothing to do with the main text of the novel. It just briefly reports the plot and interest of the book in general. It can also be regarded as an advertisement. This book will be published starting today. I will do my best to write it down without any slackness, striving to complete it in one go. In addition to the copyright belonging to Shen Bao, I also retain the right to make films. If anyone thinks that the plot in the book can be used to make a film in the future, they should first obtain my consent.

Yesterday, British and American silver fell slightly. The market situation was quite flat, and the exchange rate was frequently small. The British exchange rate was 3 yuan, 3 jiao, 9 fen, and 375. The American exchange rate was 3 yuan and 4 jiao. HSBC's listed prices rose and fell differently. The British gold increased by half a grade (125), which was 1 shilling, 11 pence, and 125. The US dollar was still 32 yuan and 625. Hong Kong increased by 25, which was 75 taels and 75. The Indian exchange rate increased slightly by half a yuan. The French franc decreased by 1 yuan. The Singapore ocean decreased by 5 qian. The Japanese ocean decreased by half a shield. The German exchange rate did not change. The domestic market was British loose and American tight, which was related to the small exchange rate. It was flat in the early morning and then seemed to be good. It fell slightly at noon.
