Total Amount of Silver Discount in December 112

The silver discount in December of this session usually sits at more than 3 qian. Market prices of a few fen and qian are rarely seen. Market prices above 4 qian are only seen for a day or two. Therefore, the total amount of silver discount for the entire day is calculated for 31 days, totaling 8 taels, 6 qian, and 5 fen. The average daily pull is less than 2 qian and 8 fen. Generally, the total interest floor is only at 8 taels and a half and 95扣. The outstanding interest may be 14 or 15 taels.

The Complicated Standard of Currency Price 113

）American Eastern Silver Company, Fei Ersheng（········

The saying that "there is a lack of gold in the world," whether it comes from the mouth of economist Gastsar Cassel or is used as conversational material by ordinary people, has become an indelible fact. At present, most countries in the world use cash gold as the basis of currency price. Since currency is necessary for life, people have a clear understanding of the value of gold. However, in fact, there is always a large amount of cash accumulated in places where industry and commerce are not prosperous, which not only loses the effect of regulating finance, but also creates a tragic fall in the economic system. In recent years, the production of raw gold has gradually decreased, while the world's demand for gold has increased by 2% per year. In contrast, it is increasingly felt that there is not enough cash to supply the basis of currency price. Therefore, the fact that gold is expensive is also undeniable. The prices of goods in various countries in the world are declining. The comparison between daily necessities such as wheat, cotton, and silver and gold is becoming cheaper. Therefore, the call for a complex bimetallic standard arises in response to the times. This is indeed enough to expand the basic position of currency price and to make the prices of goods gradually average and moderate. However, there are doubts about the authenticity of gold and silver. Once the production of silver is insufficient, it is also a serious problem. Reducing the amount of gold contained in legal currency is also a remedy. As for the latest currency price basis, the price index method should be promoted. However, there are two main difficulties: one is to index certain prices and seek a common index for a category, and the other is to weigh wages and rents and other considerations related to creating the index. Whether the index method is successful or not completely depends on the people's faith. The reason why the gold standard is at the end of its rope in the world's finances is also because it has lost the people's faith. Another example is the paper money circulating in the United States, with a cash reserve of only 40%. However, the people's faith is firm, and they believe that a 40% cash reserve meets the purpose of demand. Therefore, the credit of the currency system can be maintained. In fact, the US currency system is in line with the price index. This index is roughly divided into two parts: one part is 40% of the cash reserve, and the other part is 60% of the commercial paper issued by the US National Reserve Bank. The facts are all there. In order to plan the future development index method, it will be noticed by the public. According to the index set by the US Bureau of Labor, there is an index based on 550 prices. Each price has a certain weight, and scientific methods and profound theories are used to make it an index. However, the wholesale price index does not seem to be very suitable for the currency price standard. According to the British economist J. M. Keynes, a change in the real price must have important arguments. The employment situation, the amount of output, the bank's loan limit, the interest rate obtained from various investments, the capacity of new production, the amount of cash flow, the foreign trade statistics, and the average exchange rate must all be studied in detail. Keynes and his famous economists believe that the stability of prices is the goal of our demand. In recent years, various unfortunate attempts to fix prices have even shaken the economic status of several countries. Therefore, many people say that holding on to prices is a bad method. George Roberts of the US National Bank once advocated firmly establishing a system of individual effort, but in reality it is not very in line with the world trend. If this is to seek stability, we will become robots.

What economists call stability is not absolute. Its purpose is nothing more than to prevent special rises and falls and maintain balance. There are also one or two exceptions. For example, when short skirts are popular in the market, millions of yards of cotton cloth have no way to sell and the surplus cotton is instantly piled up into thousands of bales. Another example is that the coffee inventory is enough to supply the whole year. If someone only drinks one cup per meal, even if the surplus is sold at the lowest price, no one will care to buy it. Therefore, the rise and fall of prices, the fall of currency prices, and the theory of supply and demand are all closely related. It is said that the science of creating indexes is still very young. Several scientists are currently researching the method of creating indexes. The fundamental understanding is being changed at present. Therefore, the concept of stability will not be emphasized in the future. The world's civilization is changing with each passing day. The research on currency price standards should focus on the concept of change and ignore the old ideas of stability. At a time when the gold standard is collapsing and the situation is serious, the people's faith is also shaken. It is not easy to rebuild new faith on non-existent objects. However, the people's faith in the government is still firm. Therefore, whether the index method can be effective depends on the government's strong promotion and the people's faith.

▲ Extreme Heartache

The Shanghai Citizens' Association, in light of the national crisis, issued a special notice to all citizens yesterday to cease New Year celebrations, stating: "Regarding the matter of the notice, this year's New Year's Day coincides with the time when our Northeast Three Provinces are being completely occupied by the violent Japanese forces, due to the border defense commander Zhang Xueliang commanding his troops not to resist. All our citizens feel extreme heartache. At this time when lost territory has not yet been recovered, we should cease New Year celebrations to mark our mourning."

Feng Yuxiang's Talk

Regarding the Withdrawal from Jinzhou 126

▲ The People Must Rise Up Automatically and Expedite Action

▲ Urge the Government to Resist the Violent Japanese

After arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Feng Yuxiang left by car at 11:00 AM yesterday to visit Xu Qian, Li Liejun, Cheng Qian, and others. He then returned to his residence for lunch with Xu, Li, and others. In the afternoon, he met with reporters from various newspapers and issued a statement regarding the withdrawal of troops from Jinzhou. In the evening, he hosted a dinner at his residence, with Liu Yufen acting on Feng's behalf to invite representatives from various circles in Shanghai. It is said that Feng has decided not to leave Shanghai in the next four days, and the trip to Fenghua may not materialize. The news from yesterday is recorded below:

▲ Receiving Guests from Various Circles: At 9:30 AM yesterday, the newly appointed Director-General of Training of the National Government, Li Jishen, and the Commander-in-Chief of the Fourth Army Group, Li Zongren, visited and talked for about half an hour. After Li and others left, Zhang Zhijiang, Zhang Fakui, and others met with Mr. Feng and invited Ma Fuxiang by car to talk. After Ma arrived at 10:30 AM, Fang Zhenwu also arrived. The commissioners met for about an hour. Mr. Feng then visited Xu Qian, and Ma and others waited at his residence. He then came with Xu Qian, Li Liejun, and others and stayed for lunch. In the afternoon, Fang Zhenwu, Guo Chuntao, Liu Zhilu, Gan Naiguang, Chen Jintao, Lu Bohong, Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, Huang Jinrong, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, and Wang Hanliang from the Citizens' Association, Zou Zhongying, a representative from the Labor University, and Ni Yishi and eight other representatives from the Anti-Japanese Association of the Five Southeastern Provinces were all received by Mr. Feng.

▲ Regarding the Withdrawal from Jinzhou: At 4:00 PM yesterday,

Mr. Feng personally shook hands with reporters from various newspapers. When our reporter inquired about the withdrawal of troops from Jinzhou and the urgency of the situation in Pingjin, Mr. Feng replied, "Regarding the withdrawal of troops from Jinzhou, according to a telegram from my friend, the troops east of Jinzhou defending the area were the three brigades of Rong Zhen's department. When they were still 300 li away from the enemy, the two brigade commanders led their troops to retreat. Another brigade was also affected. When they returned to see Rong Zhen, Rong scolded them for not resisting, saying that if they were so timid, they should not be soldiers. The two brigade commanders actually said, 'If you want to resist, you go resist.' Rong was extremely angry and went to Ping to resign. This is the situation of civil and military officials today. Now that disaster is imminent, these officials cannot be relied upon. Only the people can rise up automatically to urge the government to save itself and the country." As the reporter was about to inquire further about how the people could rise up automatically, Mr. Feng hurriedly bid farewell due to his eagerness to meet other guests, saying repeatedly that they would talk in detail another day.

▲ Details of the Meeting with Wang: Mr. Feng Yuxiang issued the following statement yesterday regarding his meeting with Wang Jingwei: "(Question) What were the details of your discussions with Mr. Wang yesterday?" (Answer) "Yesterday I went to the hospital and visited Mr. Wang at his bedside. After briefly exchanging pleasantries and inquiring about his condition, I explained my ardent hope that various leaders would work together to resist foreign aggression. Mr. Wang was very indignant about the national crisis and was eager to go to Beijing as soon as possible. He said that as soon as his illness improved slightly, he would go to Beijing. At that time, the doctor came in to check his temperature and advised him to rest, so I returned home." (Question) "When will you meet Mr. Wang again?" (Answer) "The time for the next meeting will be notified by Mr. Wang, but it must be discussed with the doctor before the meeting."

▲ Expressing His Intention to Visit Hu and Jiang: When reporters visited Mr. Feng at his residence yesterday, they inquired about when he would visit Jiang Jieshi and Hu Hanmin. According to inquiries from other sources, the trip to Fenghua may be cancelled because Jiang Jieshi has indicated that he is declining guests. However, the trip to Hong Kong to meet Mr. Hu Hanmin may materialize, but Mr. Feng still needs to consider the recent situation.

▲ Denying That He Brought Plans: It was reported that Mr. Feng Yuxiang came to Shanghai to meet Wang with detailed plans for recovering the lost territories in the Northeast by force. The content was that Feng and Yan would transfer the old departments in the Northwest to the front line under a new system, with a troop strength of about 300,000 men. When reporters went to Mr. Feng's residence yesterday to inquire about whether there were such plans, Mr. Feng's secretary Gao Xinya was responsible for

replying that the above sections were completely inaccurate.

▲ Ye Bin's Visit Yesterday Morning: At 6:00 AM yesterday morning, Ye Bin, Chairman of the Standing Committee of the Shanghai Youth Volunteer Suicide Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps, went to 301 Avenue Mesny, French Concession, to visit Mr. Feng Yuxiang. Mr. Feng had been busy the previous night and had not yet gotten up. Li Weicheng received him on behalf of Mr. Feng. The following is a verbatim record of the order of questions and answers in their conversation: "(Ye asks) What kind of mission does Commander Feng have for this trip to Shanghai, and how many days will he be staying?" (Li replies) "He came to Shanghai to express his condolences to Mr. Wang Jingwei, and he will only be staying for three days." "(Ye asks) What are Commander Feng's thoughts on the recent situation in Jinzhou?" (Li replies) "He is determined to recover the lost territories by force in the near future and encourages the people of the whole country to unite and unanimously resist foreign aggression, and he will never willingly surrender an inch of territory." "(Ye asks) Since Commander Feng is determined to recover the lost territories by force, all members of our corps are willing to serve as a backing. I wonder when Commander Feng will go to Beijing, and our corps is willing to follow Commander Feng." (Li replies) "Very good, Brother will definitely convey your wishes to Commander Feng." Then, Ye Bin, the chairman of the suicide squad, presented a book of inscriptions from the group and asked Commander Feng to write an inscription for posterity.

Li Weicheng agreed to convey the request. Mr. Feng agreed to have a detailed meeting again at 6:00 AM tomorrow. Later, Xing Pu, the former councilor of the Qingdao Municipal Government, also came to visit Mr. Feng, and the chairman of the corps bid farewell and left.

▲ Zhang Qun's Banquet This Afternoon: Mayor of the city, Zhang Qun, believing

that Mr. Feng is tireless and enthusiastic about consolidating the leaders of the party and the country,

has specially arranged a banquet for Mr. Feng at the Eight Immortals Bridge Youth Association at 12:00 noon today (New Year's Day), with Kong Yongzhi, Li Xiehe, and Huang Yingbai accompanying.

▲ Inviting Mr. Feng to Speak: The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of the Five Southeastern Provinces yesterday afternoon appointed representatives to visit Mr. Feng's residence on Avenue Mesny, where they were received by Secretary He Chuqiang on behalf of Mr. Feng. The representatives of the association then stated the significance of initiating a mass meeting to welcome Mr. Feng Huanzhang to lead the people, which will be held at the public sports ground at 1:00 PM today (New Year's Day), and requested Mr. Feng to participate in the meeting, speak, and guide the people on the policy of resisting Japan. Secretary He was entrusted to convey this to Mr. Feng, and it is said that Mr. Feng has agreed to it.

▲ Talking with Liu Musu: Shanghai commercial transport representative Liu

Musu, along with Chen Weixin, director of the Road Association, and Ruan Ming, secretary of Li Renchao, visited Mr. Feng yesterday to report on the progress of the people's movement in Shanghai and to solicit Mr. Feng's policy on saving the country internally and externally. According to Liu Musu's statement, Mr. Feng's responses were as follows: "(1) Japan's forcible occupation of the Three Northeastern Provinces is like a robber entering a house with a knife. Everyone in the house should use their legs and arms and do their best to resist in unison, and perhaps they can subdue the robber to death. They must not just watch the robber enter the house and, while he is committing the crime, still want to declare that they are preparing to take up a knife to deal with him. You must know that if the knife is not properly prepared, you will be killed by the robber. What is most peculiar is that a military officer declares non-resistance. I ask, the people pay the soldiers in the hope that they will protect the country and defend the people. Now that the country is in danger, the soldiers are compromising in the hope of wealth and honor. It is better to raise chickens to lay eggs and dogs to guard the house. (2) Democratic politics must be people-oriented. I remember that during the Franco-Prussian War, the French soldiers retreated step by step for three to four hundred li. The people were filled with righteous indignation and, supporting the old and carrying the young, went to the front line to question and scold the retreating soldiers and even used weapons to attack them. As a result, the entire army was aroused and drove back the German troops three to four hundred li. Also, the Japanese people often destroy the residences of congressmen. When asked why, they said that their words and deeds do not match and they deceive our people, so they do so. The police still protect them and never interfere or oppress them. This shows that the people are automatically rising up to save themselves and the country and to supervise the government's administration and finances, or to impeach corrupt officials, which is an undeniable matter. (3) Central officials smoking opium are enjoying life, while ordinary people using opium ash to treat their parents' illnesses are violating the law. Central officials gambling are entertaining themselves and meeting health conditions, while ordinary people gambling are detained or fined. This is completely inconsistent with the spirit of national politics and should be improved as soon as possible."

Jinzhou in Critical Condition

Expressions from the National Crisis Assembly 127

▲Two telegrams from the Jiangsu National Crisis Relief Association ㈠ to Beiping

To Military Governor Yu Xiaohou, Brigade Commander Wang Yizhe, and all military commanders of the Northeast: You are all aware that the Japanese have occupied the Eastern Provinces, retreating without a fight, resulting in the loss of national dignity, an unprecedented disgrace. Recently, Jinzhou is reported to be in a state of emergency, and the enemy is advancing further. It is difficult to guess whether the commander-in-chief is determined to fight. Gentlemen, you are all patriotic men. Ask yourselves honestly, how can you face this? The people exhaust their resources to support the army, but one person surrenders to the enemy for personal gain. Which is more important, the people or the individual? Gentlemen, you are the pillars of the nation, not personal slaves. The national situation is in such dire straits that you should awaken early, make a firm decision, rise up in unity, and fight together against foreign enemies, seeking survival for the nation and preserving the honor of soldiers. Do not let General Ma Zhanshan be the only one to distinguish himself. Looking north at your banners, we telegraph this message with tears. We hope you will understand and consider it carefully. Respectfully, from Ma Liang, Feng Jiaxi, Zhao Fengchang, Han Guojun, Huang Yilin, Yao Wenxun, Wang Qingmu, Shen Enfu, Tang Wenzhi, Zhang Yiyong, Ma Shijie, Dong Kang, Zhuang Yunkuan, Li Genyuan, Xu Dingkang, Qin Xitian, Shen Weixian, Huang Qinglan, Mu Xiangyue, Lu Guiliang, Zhu Shaowen, Jia Fengzhen, Yuan Xiluo, and others of the Jiangsu National Crisis Relief Association.

㈠ To the Special Foreign Affairs Committee of the Nanjing National Government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs: During this reorganization, the national crisis is intensifying. The people endure tears and look forward to new strategies. Yet, the Japanese invaders are pressing hard, and the Jinzhou army is retreating in disarray. No real resistance is seen, and no plans to respond are heard. We still remember when the Eastern Provinces were first lost, the people were suspicious of the Minister's visit to Japan. The previous government even made critical remarks. The Minister twice stated that the trip to the East was precisely to save the Eastern Provinces. Now that the new government has been established, it should have a plan to salvage the situation and silence criticism, otherwise it will be abandoning itself. The government has a major responsibility to the people. In this time of national crisis and public anxiety, how is national defense being prepared? How will diplomacy be used to fight for our rights? How can the Eastern Provinces be saved? Please determine a major plan and announce it to the people to comfort their hopes. Respectfully, from Ma Liang, Feng Jiaxi, Zhao Fengchang, Han Guojun, Huang Yilin, Yao Wenxun, Wang Qingmu, Shen Enfu, Tang Wenzhi, Zhang Yiyong, Ma Shijie, Dong Kang, Zhuang Yunkuan, Li Genyuan, Xu Dingkang, Qin Xitian, Shen Weixian, Huang Qinglan, Mu Xiangyue, Lu Guiliang, Zhu Shaowen, Jia Fengzhen, Yuan Xiluo, and others of the Jiangsu National Crisis Relief Association.

▲Declaration of the Hunan National Crisis Relief Association to All Newspapers and the Public: The Japanese have been plotting against us for over forty years, from the Sino-Japanese War of 1894 to the forced "Twenty-One Demands" of 1915. Our people tend to forget past events, and no countermeasures have been prepared. Now, the violent Japanese are repeating their old tricks, suddenly invading and penetrating deep into our territory, occupying Liaoning and Shenyang, seizing Jilin and Heilongjiang, and recently launching a fierce attack on Jinzhou, threatening North China. They act as they please, treating us as nothing, while we are caught off guard and only known for our non-resistance. For four months since the disaster began, apart from the people boycotting Japanese goods, General Ma Zhanshan defending the territory, and students forming groups to petition, nothing else has been heard. The authorities rely on appealing to the League of Nations to shirk responsibility and appease the people. International relations and negotiations are indeed a possible tactic, but relying on this to seek survival, opening the door to welcome thieves, and waiting to be slaughtered without any resistance is incomprehensible. Now, the National Government has undergone a refreshing reorganization, yet no concrete plan to defend against the national crisis has been heard. All that is heard is that Jinzhou is in imminent danger. The trick of the monkey trainer, giving three in the morning and four in the evening, is at its wit's end. Our people are already in a desperate situation. With the nation destroyed and families ruined, disaster is imminent. We are at a crossroads, heading towards a common end. Recently, people in Jiangsu organized the National Crisis Relief Association to inspire and call upon each other to jointly avert the crisis. As the saying goes, "Though Chu has only three households, it will surely destroy Qin." Following the legacy of Jingzeng and the extraordinary achievements of Huang and Cai, we people of Hunan will certainly not lag behind in defending our country. With this spirit, we have organized the Hunan National Crisis Relief Association in Shanghai, and held its founding meeting on December 30th, declaring our aim to save the country and seek the survival of our nation. Fellow countrymen, elders, and brothers, let us work together! Telegraphing in fear, awaiting your wise guidance. Xiong Xiling, Zhao Hengti, Peng Yunyi, Cheng Zikai, Chen Qiang, Song Hegen, Cheng Songwan, Zheng Yuan, Xia Shoutian, Ye Kaixin, Wang Zhaojin, Nie Qikun, Cai Juquan, Chen Jie, Wu Jinghong, Qin Bingzhi, Zhang Yipeng, Li Shicen, Zuo Shunsheng, Liu Dazhu, Shou Bin, Liu Bai, Liu Shijie, Ouyang Ren, Yuan Huaxuan, Chen Guojun, Guo Yuanjue, Luo Dafan, Tan Daonan.

▲Telegram on behalf of the Hubei National Crisis Relief Association (Titles Abbreviated): The sudden onset of the Japanese disaster has shocked the whole country. The people are running around calling out [for help], but the government turns a deaf ear. Thousands of miles of beautiful rivers and mountains are discarded like weeds. Hundreds of thousands of soldiers are as cowardly as dogs and sheep. We have a traditional national policy, but lack consistent diplomacy, resorting to wagging our tails for pity, considering co-management as a good plan, bowing our heads to be slaughtered, seeking neutrality and temporary peace, planting the seeds of national and racial destruction, and laying the foundations for the shame of our ancestors. Yet, [the government] suppresses the people's spirit, restricts public opinion, stifles just arguments, and suddenly starts counter-revolutionary prisons, labeling righteous indignation as treason. These are all recent traces of the government and unprecedented painful history of the nation. The people are heartbroken, weeping blood, collapsing on the ground, and crying to the heavens, unable to restrain themselves. Fortunately, peace has been achieved and unification is promising. The advice of contemporary worthies is all good strategy for future reforms. If we can unite sincerely, reform ourselves, correct the wrongs of individual dictatorship, promote democratic and centralized governance, revitalize and save the country, and learn from past failures, the future of the nation will be promising. We are all citizens and have a responsibility for the rise and fall of the nation. We fear the danger of a collapsing nest and broken eggs, and dare to express our opinions. We briefly list a few points for discussion. First, politics must be absolutely transparent. In recent years, one-party rule has gradually become a dictatorship. When the people first accepted this rule, they trusted it without doubt. However, the government, holding great power, made mistakes in every action, causing increasing suspicion and endless wars, with national finances shrinking and people's livelihoods suffering. Who can excuse the blame for these mistakes? Recently, Mr. Wang Jingwei, Mr. Sun Ke and other dignitaries and elders have telegraphed, advocating either convening a national salvation conference or making politics absolutely transparent, implementing democratic centralization, breaking the one-party monopoly, concentrating talents, and jointly supporting the critical situation. In European and American political reforms, countless lives have been sacrificed and much blood has been shed. People have fought hard, striving forward and succeeding one after another, yet there is still no guarantee of success. But these gentlemen are resolving it with a few words. This is truly an unprecedented record in our country and should be sincerely supported by the people. We hope that they will treat each other with sincerity and put these words into practice, not losing the people's expectations due to changes in the environment. If they can follow this bright path and establish constitutional institutions as soon as possible, so that the people can directly participate in politics and jointly save the country, we deeply believe that no matter how difficult and dangerous the future may be, the people will rise up to jointly complete the great cause of saving the country. Otherwise, sticking to old ways and repeating past mistakes, the lesson of the boat capsizing is not far off. Gentlemen, you are intelligent and do not need much explanation. Second, diplomacy must be resolved independently as soon as possible. Ever since the violent Japanese invaded, the government has retreated step by step, surrendering rights and humiliating the country, causing daily increasing public anger. After unification is completed, it is appropriate for everyone to unite and make preparations for resistance with the determination to die, in order to reverse the decline and save the critical situation. As for how international relations and negotiations should be conducted, and what the limits of negotiation should be, the government should consult with the people openly, with internal and external support, in order to operate flexibly and win in negotiations, reversing the suspicion of private dealings and achieving effective national diplomacy. In the future, the government should not repeat its mistakes and lead itself to destruction. As for the long-standing restriction of freedom of speech, it should be thoroughly lifted as soon as possible. The arbitrary taking of finances should be actively reorganized as soon as possible. Military and civil affairs should be strictly separated, and internal wars and suicides should be absolutely prohibited. How can morale and public spirit be promoted? How can falseness and exaggeration be corrected? The people in the disaster areas must be provided with relief as soon as possible, and local autonomy must be implemented as soon as possible. All these things are fundamental plans for saving the country at present. From the people to the government, everyone should be wary of walking on thin ice and quickly start planning ahead. We have previously read the telegram from Mr. Ma Xiangbo and other elders of Jiangsu Province, which showed their views on national salvation, grand plans and great strategies, and deep insights into current ills. We express our strong agreement with this. We have established the Hubei National Crisis Relief Association without hesitation, following in your footsteps and jointly facing the crisis. Alas, if we do not destroy ourselves, who can destroy us? If we save ourselves, Heaven will surely have pity. We still have a breath, our conscience is not dead, we share the same hatred for the enemy, and we pledge to protect our country. If we receive consistent support from wise men at home and abroad, we will continue to present our views for your consideration. Respectfully presenting our heartfelt thoughts and awaiting your wise guidance. The Hubei National Crisis Relief Association bows.

Shanghai-Woosung Garrison Command

Dai Ji Sworn in Yesterday 129

▲Zhang Qun Dispatched by Central Government to Supervise Oath and Deliver Speech

After assuming his post on the 29th of last month, Shanghai-Woosung Garrison Commander Dai Ji was sworn in at his headquarters at 2 p.m. yesterday. Zhang Qun was dispatched by the Central Government to supervise the oath, and Cai Tingkai, Commander of the 19th Route Army, also attended. About 200 guests were present. Chu Minyi, Wang Xiaolai, Ye Huijun, and others delivered speeches in succession. The details of yesterday are recorded below.

▲A Glimpse of the Auditorium The auditorium is located inside the Garrison Command Headquarters, and the arrangement is very good. In the center is the swearing-in platform, with silver shields placed in front. Security is very tight in front of the auditorium and the headquarters.

▲Attendees In addition to the oath supervisor Zhang Qun and Cai Tingkai, those who attended yesterday included Central Committee member Chu Minyi, Jiang Huaisu representing the Municipal Party Committee, Qu Shounian, commander of the 78th Division, Mao Weishou, commander of the 60th Division (the former commander of the division was Dai Ji), Sun Xiwu, secretary-general of the Garrison Commander's Office of the Beijing-Shanghai Garrison Commander.

Page 22

Guo Siyan, Chief of Staff of the 19th Route Army, Deng Zhenquan, Commander of the Shanghai-Woosung Fortress, Xu Peihuang, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, Hu Hongji, Director of the Health Bureau, Shen Yi, Director of the Public Works Bureau, Huang Boqiao, Director of the Public Utilities Bureau, Song Shiheng, Director of the Arsenal, Wu Guangzong, Director of the Hydrographic Survey Bureau, Zou Bingwen, Director of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, Guo Waifeng, Commissioner of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Yan Sixiang, Director of the Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Dai Shifu, former Director of the Public Security Bureau, Chen Beisan, Chief Prosecutor of the Third Branch of the High Court. Including representatives from various agencies and groups, there were approximately 200 people.

（Inauguration Ceremony of the New Shanghai-Woosung Garrison Commander Dai Ji） （Photographed by this Newspaper）

▲Swearing-In Scene) (1) Stand at attention, (2) Play music, (3) Sing the party song, (4) Bow three times to the national flag, the party flag, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen, (5) The chairman respectfully reads Sun Yat-sen's will, (6) Silent tribute for three minutes, (7) The oath-takers take their seats, (8) The oath supervisor takes his seat, (9) Commander Chen takes his seat, (10) The guests take their seats, (11) The commander reads the oath, (12) The oath supervisor delivers a speech, (13) Commander Chen delivers a speech, (14) Guests deliver speeches, (15) The commander replies, (16) Play music, (17) Ceremony complete (fire cannons), (18) Take photos, (19) Dismissal

▲Zhang Qun's Speech Oath supervisor Zhang Qun delivered a speech, saying: "Today is the day that Dai Ji is sworn in as the Shanghai-Woosung Garrison Commander. I am very honored to represent the Central Government in supervising the oath. Commander Dai has been working in the military for more than ten years and has achieved remarkable results. This time, because Commander Xiong Tianyi was transferred to be the chairman of Jiangxi Province, the Central Government believes that the position of Shanghai-Woosung Garrison Commander is very important, so it specially appointed Dai to take on this important task. Commander Dai's ability, knowledge, and experience in military affairs are worthy of our admiration, and he will be able to fulfill his duties happily, ensure the security of the Southeast, and promote the close cooperation of the Southeast defense. Shanghai is a place where people from all over the world gather. In terms of area, there are two concessions; in terms of population, there are more than three million people; in terms of population nationality, there are residents from more than forty countries. Its importance is evident. Since the September 18th Incident, the defense of Shanghai has become even more serious. To maintain security, the three party, government, and military organs must cooperate as a whole, and all sectors must also cooperate as a whole, in order to achieve the goal of peace in the Southeast. Therefore, every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday, the three party, government, and military sectors must hold a meeting to discuss important matters related to maintaining defense. The tranquility of Shanghai depends on this. It is expected that Commander Dai will make progress in this regard after taking office, and he will be able to bear this important mission. At the same time, I hope that people from all walks of life will cooperate with the spirit of the past. This will surely make Shanghai peaceful and allow politics, diplomacy, and culture to develop accordingly. Although I have resigned from my responsibilities in Shanghai, I will still do my best to help in a private capacity."

▲Guest Speeches Among the guests, Chu Minyi, a member of the Central Committee, said in his speech: "I am very pleased to participate in Commander Dai's swearing-in ceremony today. Shanghai is located in a strategic location, and maintaining security is very important, especially during the national crisis. We must work together. After Commander Xiong resigned, Commander Chen was afraid that he would not be able to take care of both Beijing and Shanghai, so Commander Dai was appointed as the Shanghai Commander again. Zhang Mayor has already introduced Dai's history. Such a capable person will surely consolidate Shanghai's defense." Subsequently, Ye Huijun, Cai Tingkai, Wang Xiaolai, Xu Shiying, and others delivered speeches in succession, which are omitted.

▲Dai's Response Oath supervisor, comrades, fellow soldiers, I am a little sincere and fearful when taking office here today. Why? Because I came from the army. After leaving school, I joined the army and have been in charge of soldiers. I have no experience in administrative organs. Therefore, I have been delayed for several

months in the position of Garrison Commander and have not dared to take office. Especially since Shanghai is vast and the situation is complex, I feel that I am really unable to take on the responsibility. However, the Central Government's orders must be carried out. Since I have no way to get rid of it, I have to reluctantly accept it based on the military's principle of obedience being my duty. However, although my ability is limited, I am confident that I have always had a sense of responsibility. Since I have come to accept it, whether it is good or not, I must continue to do it. As for whether it is done well or not, I ask all sectors of the local community to give instructions and be tolerant. As for the speeches of the oath supervisor and several guests, I will respectfully accept them completely and put them into practice.

▲Inauguration Telegram To All Newspapers: I have received Letter No. 919 of Appointment of Simplified Appointment from the Executive Yuan of the National Government, appointing Dai Ji as the Shanghai-Woosung Garrison Commander. This is the letter. I took office in Longhua Headquarters on the 31st of this month. I am a humble soldier with a duty to carry arms. The sea frontier is a heavy responsibility, and I am in fear of the ice abyss. I humbly ask that you give me guidance so that I can follow your instructions. In addition to reporting to the Executive Yuan, I respectfully announce this. Shanghai-Woosung Garrison Commander Dai Ji bows.

Recent News from the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association 131

The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association issued an announcement yesterday regarding the extension of the deadline for registering sealed Japanese goods for another two weeks, until January 9th, saying: "The measures for handling sealed Japanese goods have been previously announced by this Association. All merchants are to come to the Statistics Section of the Investigation Department to obtain forms, fill them out, and submit them to the Statistics Section for compilation and statistics, based on which discussions will be held. Failure to fill out the forms by the deadline will be considered as private possession of Japanese goods. Announcement No. 3 also announced that the deadline would be extended to the 25th of this month. It has now been found that the deadline has passed, and the majority of merchants have not come to the Association to fill out the forms. This is a serious mistake. For the sake of caution, the Committee has decided to extend the deadline for another two weeks, from the 26th of this month to January 9th. Merchants who have not filled out the forms should quickly come to the Association to obtain and fill out the forms during the extended period and should not delay any longer. Please be aware that filling out the forms for sealing Japanese goods is a public measure that benefits all merchants and does not harm them. Please do not wait and see. Otherwise, once the deadline has passed, it will be handled as private possession of Japanese goods. This is to inform you of the situation. Please take note."

In addition, the case of inspectors Ku Shuping and Han Guangfu, who were previously falsely accused of theft by the Zhen Dahai Flavor Store in Xinkaihe for leading a team to inspect a large batch of Japanese goods and were arrested and taken to the Second Special District Court by the French Concession Police, was heard in court at 10 a.m. yesterday. Attorney Qu Zheng appeared in court on behalf of the Association to defend them, and more than ten people, including three committee members, Li Yongxiang, Zhu Xuefan, Chen Peide, and representatives from the Inspection Department, attended the hearing. After the presiding judge questioned the details of the case, he approved bail in court and scheduled the verdict for January 6th. It is said that Attorney Fei Xizhen of the Police Department also knew that the case was a misunderstanding and made some statements, which can be said to have taken care of the patriotic movement within the scope of the law. The two inspectors who were falsely accused were released immediately after finding bail. It is said that Du Yuesheng had spoken to the authorities about this case, so both parties were able to reach an understanding during the trial.

Commemorative Stamps for Martyrs Released Today 132

The commemorative stamps featuring the portraits of martyrs have now been completely printed and transported to the Directorate General of Posts. Another Response to Stopping New Year's Celebrations 133

The Minnan Association in Shanghai believed that with the Chinese troops withdrawing within the passes and the entire Eastern Provinces about to be lost, it was inappropriate to engage in revelry and dancing during this time of grief. They telegraphed an appeal to compatriots, saying: "To anti-Japanese organizations at home and abroad and compatriots across the country: In recent times, officials have been keen on seeking advancement, soliciting bribes and offering them without limit, using the excuse of sending gifts for the New Year. Those above them in rank must be congratulated, and those below them in rank will give in return. The motives of these people for celebrating the New Year are fundamentally impure. In order to improve officialdom, it should be abolished and improved as soon as possible. As for civil society gatherings, that may be a different matter, but at a time when the nation is about to fall, who is willing to force a smile? It is reported that someone advocated stopping New Year's celebrations to mark the disaster. Our Association is eager to be patriotic and has unanimously agreed. We hope that compatriots from all walks of life will no longer indulge in revelry and dancing, so as not to be accused of being unpatriotic and despised by other countries." The Minnan Association in Shanghai bows.

Completion of New Bridge Construction at Yunzaobang 134

▲Public Works Bureau Prepares for Opening Ceremony

The Yunzaobang Bridge in Woosung was in disrepair for many years, and traffic was very dangerous. The Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau planned to build a new bridge at the end of Jungong Road, west of the Woosung Railway Bridge, and drew up plans. The project was contracted to the Yujing Company of this city for a price of 87,000 yuan. Since the start of construction in mid-August of last year, it has been four months. The Public Works Bureau specially sent engineer Huang to supervise the construction in Woosung. The construction has been progressing very quickly. It is known that the construction of the bridge has been completed on schedule yesterday according to the Public Works Bureau's planned plan. Only the road surface on the south side of the bridge has not been completed, but it will be completed in about three days. It is said that the Public Works Bureau is now preparing to hold an opening ceremony on a regular basis.

Internal National Bonds Association Telegram to the Executive Yuan and Ministry of Finance 136

The Chinese Republic Internal National Public Debt Bondholders Association, yesterday sent telegrams to the Executive Yuan and Ministry of Finance, saying, (Telegram to the Executive Yuan) "Respected President Sun of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, having read your telegram from Nanjing, we respectfully acknowledge your esteemed appointment as Premier. From now on, the teachings of the late Premier will undoubtedly be fully realized one by one. We listen with admiration and extend our heartfelt congratulations. The late Premier dedicated himself to the revolution, striving for forty years, but did not complete his great task. We rely on you to inherit his legacy, tirelessly working to maintain the foundation of popular rule and save the doctrine of people's livelihood from imminent collapse. Now, facing national difficulties and the people's suffering, we hope you will embrace their pain, broadly implement plans, care for the hungry and drowning, and combine leniency with severity. Only you can be relied upon. Governing the country has myriad aspects to be addressed, but establishing trust with the people is paramount, preceding adequate food and troops. Although all policies are interconnected, establishing sound finances is the foundation for reforming all policies. Years of war and famine make increasing taxes like draining a pond to catch all the fish. Years of catching mice and digging up their nests make borrowing seem like the end of an arrow's flight. It is not easy to immediately reduce military and government expenses, and expanding construction cannot be just empty talk in the current situation. Under these circumstances, reducing expenditure and increasing revenue should follow the example of Germany, convening a national economic conference to discuss long-term plans, aiming for certainty in implementation. This would align with the late Premier's teaching of cooperation between the people and the government, and the establishment of national credit lies therein. Our association is a group of public debt bondholders, and our relationship with national policy is particularly close. Therefore, we especially offer our congratulations and humbly offer our views. In closing, we express our sincere prayers. The Chinese Republic Internal National Public Debt Bondholders Association respectfully bows and seals. (Telegram to the Ministry of Finance) Respected Minister Huang of the Nanjing Ministry of Finance, having read the news, we respectfully acknowledge your esteemed appointment as Minister of Finance. We extend our heartfelt congratulations. You have specialized in economics and have extensive knowledge of national finance. You will undoubtedly be able to make ample arrangements for national expenditure and carefully consider the burden on the people without fail. We can foresee grand plans greatly benefiting the people's livelihood. Since the founding of the Republic, finances have not been on the right track. Excessive and miscellaneous taxes have been layered upon each other, and public debt bonds have come one after another. The people are struggling to cope, and the government is exhausting its resources. Fortunately, the National Government has established its capital in Nanjing, adhering to the teachings of the late Premier, implementing the reduction of customs duties and proceeding with tax increases. The policy regarding public debt bonds is based on financial principles, with a designated fund and custody by people's representatives, and principal and interest are paid on schedule according to regulations. Therefore, in just four or five years, the amount of bonds has reached 100 million, circulating freely in the market without obstruction and stored safely among the people without fear. Unfortunately, most of the funds are used for military expenses and little for construction. Now that unification is complete and the new government is established, the national needs are vast in this time of urgent national crisis. However, with thorough reorganization, there may still be ways to increase revenue and reduce expenditure while ensuring national debt. Addressing immediate needs should begin with a financial conference, and establishing a foundation should resemble the group's economic conference. Our association is organized by bondholders and is closely related to national finance. Therefore, we dare to speak out after offering our congratulations, not avoiding overstepping our bounds, but rather offering a humble contribution. In closing, we express our hopes. The Chinese Republic Internal National Public Debt Bondholders Association respectfully bows and seals."

Transit Customs Declaration Industry Conference

Opposition to the New Customs Declaration Form 138

▲Also Opposing Business License in Management Regulations

The entire transit customs declaration industry in this city, recently due to the new customs declaration forms issued by the Jianghai Customs, scheduled to be implemented on January 5th, and the newly issued business license management regulations, are considered unusually harsh and difficult to comply with. They have successively requested a meeting to make a public decision. Therefore, yesterday (the 31st) at 3:00 PM, a general meeting of the industry was held at the Customs Declaration Association on Penglai Road in the Nanshi area. 178 companies attended, totaling over 200 people. Shi Zikun was publicly elected as chairman, who immediately reported the purpose of the meeting, inviting attendees to express their opinions. Representatives from the industry, including Zhang Qingqing, Lin Youzhang, Zhou Jing, and others, successively rose and stated that the new customs declaration forms issued by the customs had many omissions, such as the tax number and the total declaration number, which were previously filled out by customs officials and could not be handled by customs declaration firms. Furthermore, the form grids were small, the items were numerous, and the time limit was short and strict. Errors would result in penalties, making it impossible for the industry to undertake the completion. If the customs insisted on customs declaration firms completing the forms, the industry would lack the time and manpower. They would rather sacrifice business and refuse to comply. The repeated establishment of penalty clauses by the customs was also unbearable. Although the association had previously requested the Ministry of Finance to ban Japanese customs declaration firms in order to maintain national rights, the Ministry of Finance ignored it. Not only did it fail to protect them, but it issued harsh regulations instead, which was truly outrageous. Although the customs declaration industry was a small-scale operation, it did not default on customs duties. Now, requiring a large security deposit was difficult to bear. These harsh regulations were equivalent to sentencing the customs declaration industry to death. Rather than perishing together, it would be better to suspend business. After discussion among the representatives, they unanimously requested the chairman to protest to the customs authorities and withdraw the order. If the goal was not achieved, they would all suspend business. Subsequently, Chairman Shi Zikun used gentle words to persuade the representatives not to act rashly. Customs declaration firms were involved in transportation, which was related to commerce and finance, and careful consideration was necessary. They should not rely on youthful courage, which could affect the overall situation. However, the public sentiment was angry, and the words were not well received. It was resolved that if the Jianghai Customs could not understand and cancel the new customs declaration forms and harsh management regulations by January 4th, the entire industry would voluntarily strike and suspend business starting on the 5th. Everyone unanimously raised their hands, signed, and passed the resolution. The meeting ended at over 7:00 PM.

National Anti-Japanese Salvation Association Established 139

The Chinese National Anti-Japanese Salvation Association held its founding meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM in the association's auditorium. Eighteen preparatory committee members attended. Yu Ying was elected chairman and reported on the preparation process. Then, Ling Xiaoxia explained the organizational outline and made slight revisions. Subsequently, Yu Ying, Huang Xiang, Zhou Bin, Ling Xiaoxia, Lu Yiwen, and others were elected as standing committee members, and Zhang Gongliang, Zheng Qihua, Sun Chaoping, Mo Jieru, Xing Jianyue, and others were elected as supervisory committee members. Yu Ying was also elected as chairman of the committee. Ling Xiaoxia was then appointed to draft the general meeting's telegram. Items discussed included: 1. Organizing a military affairs committee. Resolved and passed. 2. Jointly establishing five major departments: general affairs department, staff department, adjutant department, training department, and compilation department. Resolved and passed. 3. Candidates for each department would be elected by vote at the second meeting. Resolved and passed.

Local Militia Appeals to Join the Anti-Japanese War 140

The Chinese Republic National Salvation Army, prepared by Li Jianhong, Ma Hongtu, Fan Youmin, Zhou Zhigang, and others for the past three months, has made considerable progress. Li Jianhong and Ma Hongtu were publicly elected as commanders of the first and second divisions, respectively. Now that the Japanese invaders are pressing on and Jinzhou is in danger, continuing to resist without fighting will inevitably lead to national demise. Yesterday, an emergency meeting was convened, and it was unanimously agreed to request General Zhang Fakui to lead troops north to kill the invaders as soon as possible.

Overseas Chinese National Salvation Association Established Today 141

The Overseas Chinese National Salvation Association, initiated by Xie Fuchu, chairman of the current Overseas Chinese Industrial Advancement Association, has been actively preparing and is now ready. It is scheduled to hold its founding meeting today at No. 2 Zhenxin Nanli, Dongxin Bridge Street, Fada Road. Yesterday, the preparatory office issued a notice stating that since the outbreak of the Liaoning Incident, three months have passed, and the entire country is filled with anger. Although the overseas Chinese have resided in foreign lands for a long time and engaged in business overseas, they have not forgotten their homeland and still cherish their patriotic hearts. They dare not lag behind in the grand undertaking of national salvation. Therefore, based on public opinion, the Overseas Chinese National Salvation Association is organized in Shanghai, and responsible personnel have been designated to actively prepare. It has been submitted to the National Government for filing and will begin operations on New Year's Day of the 21st year of the Republic. Saving the nation with iron and blood is a shared aspiration. The association hopes that patriotic compatriots at home and abroad and wise authorities will provide assistance to overcome the great difficulties together.

Japanese Detectives

Arrest and Escort of Korean Communist Leaders 142

▲Gu Ranqun and Wen Shanzai

▲Escorted from Shanghai to Korea on the Shanghai Maru

Korean Communist Party leader Gu Ranqun, who was arrested in Shanghai last year, was detained in Shanghai. His party work was then carried out by his secretary, Wen Zongmiao. This time, he was arrested by Japanese detectives for planning to hold a meeting in Shanghai. Along with Gu Ranqun, who had been arrested earlier, he was escorted to Japan and then to Korea. The details of this incident are as follows:

▲The Escort of Gu Ranqun Gu Ranqun, a Korean, served as a staff member in the statistics section of the Central Headquarters and as a political worker in the Military Police Corps after graduating from the Huangpu Military Academy. After being dismissed, he came to Shanghai and joined the Communist Party. He was responsible for the electric extraction sent by the Seoul District Court of Korea and sent to Korea for interrogation.

▲Wen Zongmiao's Activities After Gu's arrest, the position of guiding member of the Korean Communist Party was taken over by Gu's secretary, Wen Shanzai (also known as Wen Zongmiao), who was appointed by the Communist Party. He traveled between China and Korea and contacted Koreans in Shanghai to carry out communist work. Wen Shanzai lived in the French Concession. After receiving a secret report, the Japanese consulate had long wanted to arrest him, but his whereabouts were uncertain, making it difficult to capture him.

▲Japanese Detectives' Pursuit Recently, Wen Shanzai, under the orders of the Communist Party headquarters, was going to Ruijin, Jiangxi, to report on the progress of his work and guidance. He first summoned the Korean Communist Party members under his leadership in Shanghai to a meeting in a house between Zhaopu Road and Tianmu Road to report on everything and instruct them on future work. However, he was detected by Japanese detectives, who ambushed a large number of detectives on Zhaopu Road on the 26th of this month, intending to capture them all at once. Wen also received the news and did not dare to go. Later, he disguised himself and went to Hongkou alone to scout the situation, but was arrested by Japanese detectives and taken to the Japanese Consulate.

▲Transfer to Korea After Wen Shanzai was arrested, he was interrogated by the judicial section of the Japanese Consulate. It was learned that he was directly in contact with the Communist Party headquarters in Jiangxi Province and was the leader and instructor of the Communist Party throughout Korea. The Japanese considered this case extremely important, and Gu Ranqun was also an important member of the Communist Party. When the Seoul District Court extracted Gu Ranqun, the Japanese Consulate sent several Japanese police officers to escort Gu and Wen on the Shanghai Maru to Kobe and then to Korea for a joint trial. When the two prisoners, Gu and Wen, boarded the ship, the wharf was heavily guarded. After boarding the ship, they were locked in separate rooms to prevent escape.

Postal Workers Everywhere Request Promulgation of Special Trade Union Law 143

The Shanghai Postal Workers' Union, Rural Workers' Union, and the postal workers' unions of Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, and other places, jointly submitted a report to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Transportation, and the Legislative Yuan, stating that: "We respectfully request the prompt promulgation of the Special Trade Union Law so that there is a law to follow and it benefits the labor movement. Our unions were organized in accordance with the Trade Union Organization Regulations personally drafted by the late Premier in 1924 and the Special Trade Union Organization Regulations of 1928. Postal workers in various places have also successively organized. The establishment of our unions did not lack a legal basis at the beginning. However, after the success of the revolution and the establishment of the capital, the provisions of Article 3 of the Trade Union Law of 1929 and the cancellation of the Special Trade Union Organization Regulations of 1930 caused the already established special trade union organizations in various places to lose their legal basis, causing confusion among postal workers across the country. The party headquarters in various places felt that guidance was difficult and successively requested explanations. They were pleased to think that there would be a day when a special trade union law would be promulgated for special industries, and people's hearts turned to a certain direction. Unexpectedly, the Implementing Regulations of the Trade Union Law passed on May 25, 1930, had ambiguous wording and difficult to fathom intentions after detailed explanations. Delayed until now, the postal unions in various places, with a close relationship and deep love, still maintain their original organizations. However, with the strictness of the law, how can they conflict with it? With the importance of union affairs, how can they be allowed to wander? Therefore, they have repeatedly expressed their concerns to the Executive Yuan and Ministry of Transportation. We now submit a draft of the Special Trade Union Law and respectfully request that the Executive Yuan and Ministry of Transportation approve the prompt promulgation of the Special Trade Union Law based on the Trade Union Organization Regulations personally drafted by the late Premier in 1924 and the Special Trade Union Organization Regulations promulgated in 1928, so that the original good organizations of postal workers can be further consolidated and serve the party and the country faithfully. We also request that when drafting the law, our unions be allowed to send representatives to attend, fully express our opinions, and benefit the people's will and the effectiveness of the law. We await your urgent orders."

Four Labor Regulations Announced in This City 144

The labor regulations in this city, after the implementation of the Factory Law, were explicitly abolished by the Municipal Government. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau separately drafted the Small Factory and Commercial Shop Employee Rules that are not applicable to the Factory Law. It also drafted the Worker Treatment Rules, Worker Service Rules, Commercial Shop Employee Service Rules, and Commercial Shop Employee Treatment Rules and submitted them for approval. They have been amended and passed by the 198th Municipal Government Meeting and were instructed yesterday to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for compliance and promulgation.

Collection of Land Survey Fees 145

The Shanghai County Government was ordered by the province to conduct land surveys and collect a land survey fee of one dime per mu (unit of area). However, this year's floods in this province have been particularly severe, and the people's livelihood has been devastated. Wujin and other counties have successively requested extensions to alleviate the people's suffering. It was subsequently approved that those with a harvest of 50-60% or less would be granted a one-year extension to alleviate the people's suffering. This county is not on the list of extensions, so the Finance Bureau has already received from the County Government the land survey fee receipt format issued by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance and ordered compliance.

Overview of German Trade with China from January to September Last Year 146

▲Trade Deficit of 54 Million Marks

According to statistics from the German financial authorities, German exports to China from January to September 1931 totaled 100.9 million marks, while imports from China totaled 160.3 million marks, resulting in a trade deficit of 54 million marks.

Bank of China Inspection Report 147

▲Forty-Sixth

The forty-sixth inspection report of the Shanghai Bank of China Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee stated that the committee members and entrusted accountants, in accordance with the committee's rules, inspected the Shanghai Bank of China's issuance and interbank exchange coupon reserve treasury. The forty-sixth inspection was held at the bank on December 27, 1931, and the Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance joined the inspection. The inspection results are listed on the left: the total amount of exchange coupons issued was 123,493,968 yuan, including 64,188,570 yuan issued by the bank, 29,573,574 yuan used by interbanks, and 29,731,824 yuan used by various banks and firms. In addition to the portion used by various banks and firms being inspected separately according to the original method, this inspection focused on the interbank portion as follows: the amount issued by the bank and used by interbanks was 93,762,144 yuan. The amount of exchange coupon reserve for the bank and interbanks was 93,762,144 yuan, including 56,511,606.79 yuan in cash reserve and 37,250,537.21 yuan in guarantee reserve. The above two items, with the cash reserve accounting for 60% and the guarantee reserve accounting for 40%, were all checked as accurate. In accordance with Rule 5, this is a formal report. December 27, 1931, representatives of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce: Pei Yunqing, Wang Yansong; representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association: Hu Mengjia, Wu Lan; representatives of the Shanghai Money Dealers Association: Yan Junan, Ji Jisheng; representatives of the coupon receiving banks and firms: Liu Hongyuan, Hu Jisheng; Bank of China supervisory board representatives: Zhou Zongliang, Dong; accountant: Wang Zikang.

▲Advocating Strict Opium Prohibition

▲Fighting the "Long Life Paradise" Case
